O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	Oh you, dear son, I have completed this book which is the last of medical science and together with its fulfillment and at its end through its exposition and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete this treatise with this section, which is part of the work on hands, namely "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work on hands is practiced in our region and employed everywhere entirely, it has been completely forgotten except for small descriptions found in ancient books where hands have moved them.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And thus comes the mistake and arrogance, with minds closed and wisdom forsaken.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	 Or I believe that to revive it, you should follow the treatise's guidance on exposure and explanation as well as abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	 And I shall also use the forms of fire cauldrons and other instruments for surgery, with the assistance of preparation and explanation as necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no good masters are found in our time, the art of medicine has been abandoned.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	by and ou bonte;sso ça que t1: s.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	 And so Hippocrates says that one without knowledge is much, but with effort it is little.
et meismement en l’art de main.	 and especially in the art of surgery.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	 We tell you in the introduction to this book that those who are not attentive to what has been said before will err and may kill people.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	 thus I have wanted many times more from those who engage in this knowledge, yet abandon the theory and lack experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	 For I saw a mad barber who cut an abscess of scrofulous swellings or the neck of a woman, and severed the arteries in her neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	 for this is why so much blood issued that the woman died between his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	 And I saw another barber who treated a stone in a man's eye, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	 if he carried away with him a part of the bladder, and he died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I had already been called to extract it, and see the position of the patient and the size of the stone, and if one were to cut into it, he would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	 And I saw another barber who took care of a duke from our land who had his leg broken, and with the fracture there was an injury;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	 and the ignorant barber strained the fracture near to the injury with strong ligatures, did not allow any bandage on the wound, and left it like this for termination.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	 And he commanded that they should not dislocate at all;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	 and remain so, lest the leg becomes entirely numb and useless, leading to ruin.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	 I am called upon for treatment, and you hurry to come and reset my dislocated leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	 and when it is set right as I hear, it becomes at peace, feeling no pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	 But in any case, the contagion had already taken hold or limb, and could not be healed;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	 and the contamination did not cease until it spread through the limb completely lost all function.
Et vis .i. autre mire qui effondra .i. apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And behold a different physician who collapsed an abscess that became inflamed due to the illness of its lordship.

Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	 And therefore, dear son, you must know that this art of healing is divided into two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	 namely, where there is danger in various conditions.
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	 And I will show, at each location of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	 For that's why you must be cautious, so the foolish may not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	 If you take up your weapons in combat, and approach your illnesses easily yet firmly, and choose the best course so that by God's grace you are healed and praised.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	 And let not grave diseases bring distressing health;
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	 And use your weapons as you doubt their effectiveness, and have faith in yourself to come from this world of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	 Galien occasionally gave these warnings:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	 "Do not take in care of diseases badly, that you are not called foolish doctors.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	 "I have devised this treatise in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	 The first chapters are about the fire cautery and cold medicinal cauteries, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	 And about suppurations, and iron cauterizations, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	 The second chapter is about tailoring and cutting, and of cupping and wounds, and extracting arrowheads, and such matters.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	 And it is the chapter ordered with the forms of inflammations.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	 The third chapter concerns resetting dislocations and twists, and similar things;
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	 And it is ordered for the neck up to the head, and forms of inflammation.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	Thus we recall our work, it is necessary that I describe the nature and harm of each constitution.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	 I say that the quality of assistance, and harm caused, is the longest word and subtle science with secret solutions.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	 and on this spoke many wise men, and agreed to this;
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	 and I leave little of their words because I repeat the lengthiness.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	 I say that cauterization helps all conditions where there is material, for two types of constitutions;
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	 That is to say, hot temperament inclined towards matter, and dry temperament inclined towards matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	 In hot and dry temperament together with substances, some consider that fire cautery is greatly helpful.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	 and others said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	 that cautery is not effective for diseases arising from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	 Because the nature of fire is hot, and it should not be used to treat diseases caused by heat or dryness.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	 and those who argue the contrary say that fire cautery greatly helps diseases of heat and dryness that affect the bodies of people.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	When you examine the body of the man and his moisture to its nature by fire, you find the body cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	Because I have found it never once through experimentation.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	 And anyway, only those who have tried it and know the procedure of fire cautery through long experience, as well as the different temperaments of people, their conditions and causes of illnesses, outcomes, and time frame.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	 We have no fear of other conditions except for cold and damp illnesses.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all healers gathered and agreed on the use of fire cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know this, my son, that fire cautery is a secret of healing and has greater kindness than burning medicinal caustic.

Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	 Hot medications come from one body part to another by joining together, and bring about serious healing diseases in the affected member.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	 and sometimes it kills the patient.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	 The phosphorus does not do this due to its potency or goodness of its nature unless there is an excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	 And this I found through experimentation and the longevity of my service and study in the art, which is on the truth of things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	 and therefore I excuse myself for the length of my words because it is not my desire to withhold from you the secret which lies in heat or fire, and the quality of the work as how it overcomes diseases of the body, as the philosopher demonstrates.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	 Or receive them into your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, when to perform cauterizations, they seek advice from learned men.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	 And I say that cautery is appropriate at all times, because the harm occurring can be avoided with the aid of cautery.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	 and particularly when cautery is needed urgently for pains that cannot wait until a more serious harm comes to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	 And never think like foolish monks; 
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	 For the disease treated by fire cautery has no recurrence.
et il le dient ensi;	 and it heals in this manner;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	 but it is not as they think, for cautery is a medicine that changes the complexion and dries the humors causing pain, and works to quicken its effectiveness, and due to the virtue of its work and authority.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	 And things that cause disease can come at any time according to the complexion of the patient and their condition and its power;
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	 And they are combined in him due to the acquisition of meats and other things, unless cautery is administered where there is little excess and moisture, as with cautery for pain, and other things, so that pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	 But little of this happens often.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	 And many people do not understand why fire cautery is considered the last resort in medicine, and that's clear.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	 But they do not believe that fire cautery is valid after medicine; however, their understanding is false, and it's considered the last resort in medicine because when we administer treatments for any illness and they prove ineffective, then we apply fire cautery, which does work.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Then it is well understood that cauterizations are the last of medicine, not according to the foolish beliefs of some people.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	 The ancients said that a gold instrument for fire cautery is more effective than iron, and they claimed this due to the quality of gold and the preciousness of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	 and they said that the heat of fire canguary does not cause harm, but this is incorrect as I have tested it myself and found in some men.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	 And gold cauterization is preferred over iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	 However, when you heat the instrument of gold, you do not know if it has been heated by the color of the gold, and so soon cools.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	 and if it is overheated.
si font au feu;	 and they make it in fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	 And thus there are enough hindrances.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And for this reason we use fire cautery because we have found its application to our work useful.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Now I have ordered this chapter from head to toe, so that the path may be easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	The olive oil caustic
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	These cauterizations are for moisture and cold in the brain; those which are done due to a disease called "soda," and by many humors descending to the head, ears, causing numerous dreams and pain of teethache and throatache, especially for all diseases that come from coldness such as paralysis, stroke, apoplexy, and similar illnesses.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	 The form of this cautery is such that the patient may be purged by a solvent medicine affecting either part III or IV, depending on what the properties and nature and habits of the sick person can tolerate.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	 And then make sure to raise the head of the sick person.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	 And then you should have them sit with their crossed legs between your hands, and place their feet on a pillow.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	 afterwards put the base of your palm over the base of his neck between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	 and when it comes to your two methods, if there is bleeding from the wound then quickly apply the caustic called "olivary," of which this is the form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	 And he makes it touch at its place with his finger, and do so by drawing and straining your hand little by little while turning.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	 Then gently lift your hand immediately, and adjust the place where you see the small bone.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	 And if you do not see it, continue the cauterization until you see the bone as I have told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	 After taking a little bit of wool, and placing moist and soft cotton inside, then puts it at the place, leaving it for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	 Then put on butter-soaked fine cotton.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 And leave until the burned area is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After, cleanse the wound with an ointment called 'tetrapharmacist', until it is healed.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	 And the ancients say, when a wound is open longer, it cleanses more.
et por ce si aide mues.	 Therefore, to facilitate healing.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And some say that one must thoroughly clean the fire cautery if a part of the bone is burnt, and then repair what has been burned from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	 And others say that the cautery should be applied as much as possible, and pushed in so hard to widen the opening like the pins women use in their hair for the humours to come out.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	 and one must keep the open wound exposed for a long time.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	 After this, it should be cleaned and bandaged.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	 And these two methods of cauterization do not seem to be good in all cases except for some men where there is fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	 and I think that it would be best to leave them.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	 For the head becomes weakened by continuous exposure to bodily fluids, as we testify with other limbs.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	 Similarly, when the head is weak due to its natural state, and the initial sign of a caustic burn seems more healing for me, I undertake this work accordingly with greater benefit.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	From the pain at the nape of the neck to severe headache
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	 When pain persists in the entire head and lasts for a long time, the patient must use years and pills called "cachia," as well as cleansing of the head and oils and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	 And if one performs the caustic treatment that we have previously mentioned, it proves effective.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	 Be mindful if the patient's headache is of strong nature and not too cold.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	 Then you must cauterize from that cautery a little as we have said above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	 After performing cautery on each horn of the head up to the bone, as we have said before, and then perform the cautery where it is called "veins".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	 and are the places in which you apply cups.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	 and lift your hand so that it does not come up to the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	 the patient feels much greater pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will speak of elsewhere.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	 and it is proper that the cautery of the horns be more delicate than those used to cauterize the middle part of the head, which is the form.
dou cautere dou chief	For both fire cautery of the head
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	 When sudden pain occurs in one part of the head and extends throughout the body until evening, and the head is purged by various medicines, and other treatments I have mentioned in the classification of diseps, none of it helps.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	 Then you make cauteries according to two methods, namely medicinal quinsy and fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	 The cauterization of quinsy is that you pull out a strip of skin and remove the bark with the two edges, and then create an incision where the pain is most intense so that you can place the strip of skin back under the skin.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	 and when it has been replaced, if it is tied and held tightly, leave it thus for twelve hours.
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	 then you untie and treat the strip of skin, and let the wound heal for two or three days.
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	 then place a clean cloth soaked in butter until pus comes out.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 After the poultice, leave it until healed.
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	 And if you see, use some of the written or divided treatises on burning medicines that I have composed.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	 The caulteries of iron are done in this manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Heat the iron cautery with which there is the shape.
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	 And it is called "closed" because the head has been shaped like a bell or has a small protrusion, and within, there's a slight appearance.
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	 and you place it gently back into its original position, and with your hand turn the fragment slightly, until a quarter of the edge that is curved is smoothed.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	 and hold your hand so that the artery does not burn within, which is further; let plenty of blood flow.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	 After placing cotton on the wound, apply it to the area for three days;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then you place soft cotton soaked in fat on it, and then treat the area with ointment until it is healed.
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	 And if you decide to perform cauterization for this headache using the cautery called "cutellar" at its tip, and be careful not to burn the artery in such a headache which is not ancient.
de emigraine	Migraine
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	 When treating headaches as we have described in the division of diseases, and it does not work alone, and you see that the previous medicine and iron do not suffice, then it is necessary to heat the cautery called "cutellar" until it is white.
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 and gently press it on the painful area with half a finger's length of thread, and remove your hand once, ensuring you do not puncture the artery nor reach to the bone.
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	 Guard the mandible so it moves when bitten, and ensure the nerves only have regard to movement and do not cause spasms in the patient, and guard against blood flow from the artery when it is severed or cutting into it causes great fear and especially for those who are unaware of it and untrained.
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	 Leave your hand along the path;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	 But I will tell you how to stop blood when an artery is cut, and I will show you there where it takes place in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	 And if you see that this cautery does not ease the illness at all and the patient is suffering, cauterize it between the skull as we have said, and heal the wound until it is healthy.
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	 And if you see it, apply the fire cautery as described in the extraction of the artery chapter, using the cautery that has two blades.
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	 and this type of cauterization is better than that one and more helpful.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	From the pain of ears caused by coldness
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When pain from coldness comes to the ear, and we have applied soluble medicines and other treatments as mentioned in the division, and the pains do not cease, then heat this cauterizer called "points," of which here is the form:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	 After making an incision all around the ear of the patient, where both sides hold pain, and then move away slightly above the root of the ear once you have secured the opening.
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	 and make it 10 points around each ear.

de la torture de la bouche	Regarding the torment of the mouth
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	 Pain that must be treated with fire cautery includes only those caused by moisture, as we have mentioned in the division of diseases.
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	 And do not perform a fire cautery on wounds caused by scratches or nerve swelling.

l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	 One at the root of the ear, another slightly behind the temple, and the third between the two lips.
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	 Place the fire on the healthy part of it and make the first fire at the top of the ear just a bit behind the tip of the head, and another one on the temple as long as a piece.
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	 And let the fire remain until half of its color is burned off.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 And this is the form of the fire cautery:
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	 And it is a similar method to the knife treatment that we have described before, but it requires that the knife be slightly larger.
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 after curing them as I have mentioned before, until they are healed.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	 When apoplexy is ancient and you treat it as we have said, and there is no improvement, and the patient has no fever, then perform four fire cauteries:
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	 Two on the two horns of the head, one in the middle, and one where it is called "vessels" as we have said before, and then a fire cautery at the mouth of the stomach.
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	 And so treat as we have said before.
de litargie	From lethargy

de la froidor dou chief	From coldness of the head
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	 It is necessary to cleanse the head of hairs and dirt, as we have previously said;

de l’epilempsie	Of epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	The epileptic should not use a strong fire cautery except for those who are phlegmatic, and first it is necessary to purify the brain with herbs and other treatments we have described in the section when patients are large and suffering greatly from medical treatment.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	 And if it is a child who cannot endure it, they should have gargling and chewing with medicinal substances to often cleanse the brain with good meats.
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	 After removing the child's head from the cradle, and they make the caustic as we have said before, and on each horn.

Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie.	When caused by melancholy are the excesses or corrupted moisture and large phlegm, then one should apply our described fire cauldration on those with paralysis.
Et se par la cause de melancolie est li superfluitez declinans a melancolie, et est li cors dou malaide moistes, adonc li done a boivre chose par coi li cervelz soit mundifiez, selonc ceu qu’il est devant en la division.	And if caused by melancholy are the diminishing excesses leading to melancholy, and the body is a weakly moist corpse, then give it something to drink so that the brain may be clarified, as determined by its status in the classification.
Aprés reis lou chief dou malaide;	 After raising the patient's head

aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	 after applying the ointment, use old sheep butter to move it;
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	 and heat the cloth briefly, so that they may pour warmth into themselves if possible.
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	 after emptying the circle from within the head, let it cool down.
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and do this to each patient once a week with good management until they are healthy.

et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	 and then place on cotton wool in butter and chicken fat.
de l’awe des eulz	For the healing of the eyes
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	Firstly, address the issues with the eyes as I have described in the division; then begin by having the patient drink things that purify the mind and guard against all dampness, and make them sweat or bathe several times on an empty stomach.
Aprés li comande a rere son chief, et li fai cautere emmi le chief, et li fai II cauteres sus les II temples se li dessendemens de l’awe est as II eulz ensamble, ou en I se li dessendemens est en I;	 After he commands to support his head, and makes fire cautery in the middle of the head, and makes two cauldrons over the forehead near the ears together, or one wherein the dislocation is.
et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	 and cuts out all veins and arteries that are from the crown, making the cauldrons long according to the width of the forehead.

dou cors des larmes	Doubtless this refers to "douleurs" (pains) associated with the body. Perhaps a mistake in transcription, and should read "douloureux".

de coi ci est li forme:	 of which there is the shape.

et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	 and do not leave the hand except until one-third of the paper is scorched, according to the manner I have described.
dou poil qui point l’oil	by:t;
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	 Never does it happen that hairs become gray and prick the eyelids, and there are made fire treatments in two ways:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	 This is to know of fire, or of burning medicine.

et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	 And if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so that they do not move until they grow.

puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Then he applies softened cotton wool and musk of persea sap to the oil, then uses a fire cautery which has this shape:
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit;	 After the area under the wound you have marked has been cauterized many times over, ensure that the hair is burned at that spot.

And the patient's head should be upright and their eyes showing on both sides of the medicament, and press gently with your thumb each time the patient feels a tingling from the medicine, as it tingles like fire.

Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	 When the bite marks have passed, raise the affected area and check if it has swollen as though lifted by fire or cut with an incision.
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	 And if so, that is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	 But if not, reset the medication on the affected area or if the medication has not worked, until your actions are equal and your eyes are sharp.

Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	 And if you need to protect your work thoroughly with great care so that none of the medicine gets into the eyes.

aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 After the treatment until healed;
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	 And it is the form of the bellows with the mist:

de la cure de fistule par cautere	In treating a fistula by means of cautery.
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When treating a f지stula as we have mentioned in the division of diseases, and if your treatment does not yield results, then it is necessary that you perform cautery according to this manner.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	 Command the patient to put his head in your hand;
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	 and instruct the assistant to place the physician's head between their hands so that it does not move or drop.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	 after placing soft cotton in an egg-cup or juice of parsley over the wound;
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	 then heat the cautery that is to be used.
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	 and place it close to his head as if like a feather of a dove, with the caustic being attached. (This might be referring to positioning the hot iron near the area for treatment)
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	 If you observe it, ensure it is properly aligned from top to bottom, and if you see it, make sure it is also straight like a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	 However, this must be moved for your treatment.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	 After pressing the abscess if it is open, and treating the pus, then drying it out.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	 And if it is closed, work on making an opening, and treat with a poultice.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	 After applying the hot caustic well, and hold your hand on the caustic to the painful part above the wound, so that your hands do not go mad.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	 And place the caustic in the fat of the wound, and let it rot.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	 If you approach the beginning of the fire cautery up to the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	 If not, repeat the caustic once more, and otherwise if needed, and leave for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	 Afterward, place on cotton and grease it with butter, and treat the dried ointment until it is cleaned, and after forty days pass that it has been cleansed, then apply medicinal vinegar until the bone is uncovered.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	 And follow this as what comes in your chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	 And there is a method of fire cautery for fistula that none of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	 Begin with an abscess, and lay the clay on it.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	 Afterward, put in the small split which is its form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	 and make into the quantity of one rubber of clay;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	 and hold your hand or abscess firmly, and do not move the patient at all until the softened clay flows into its place.
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	 And it is proper to put on the oil for the ill person with cotton and egg white or in water;
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	 The place of the wound is at the lower part of the anus, and it heals with a miraculous health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	 And if the abscess is healed by the cautery as we have said, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	 If not, if it must administer a drain through the vein, and return the abscess to its proper place in accordance with where it truly belongs.
des crevaices en levres	For bleeding in the lips.

de l’aposteme de la goule	; by themi;
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	 When an abscess occurs at the root of the throat or in the ear, or on the roots of the teeth, after decay and pus formation, it becomes aged and turns into a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	 And you should treat it as we have described in sections, but it does not improve.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	 Then it is necessary to apply the fire cautery according to the quantity of the furture.

dou movement des dens	By the slight movements of the teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	 When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you heal them with medicine but it is not effective, then place the patient's head in your hands.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	 after cooling the fire cautery so that you will later apply it in such a way as to place a chain on the tooth. (Note: "cainn" is an archaic term for "chain" or "loop," which could also mean a tool used for holding something in place.)
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	 Et place dans le cautère chaud hâtivement, et tende ton bras de manière à ce que le malade ressente la chaleur arrivant à la base du dents.

Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in this manner the tooth that was moving is fixed, and the gums are softened and held still, and the infected moisture dried out.
de la dolor des dens	Of tooth pain
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	 Lorsque la douleur aux dents survient par raideur ou chaleur, et que le traitement médical n'est pas efficace, alors il faut procéder à un cautérisation selon les deux méthodes :
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	 Et cautère d’huile et cautère par le feu.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	 Pour la cautérisation à l'huile : prenez de la graisse de veau, et faites-en un bouchon dans lequel vous pouvez insérer une cuillère de fer ou d'argent ;
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	 After taking cotton and wrapping it around the tip of a tent, apply butter-like meal on the sore tooth quickly, and hold it in place until it is cooled.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	 And often enough until its virtues reach the root of the tooth; if you see butter-like meal on linen and cotton that has been cooled, apply it to the aching tooth and keep it there until heat comes to the closure of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	 The fire cautery is such that you take an iron or copper vessel, and it should be large enough so the heat does not reach to the patient's mouth.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	 After heating the cautery, wait for it to cool down afterwards, and apply it to the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery has cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	 Often do this, for the pain will persist on the same day or the next.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	 And it is necessary that the patient fills his mouth with good butter during the procedure of this cautery and then let it rest.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and thus are the forms of this cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	 And perform a cautery on the eyelid you wish to, according to what you can afford.
et c’est li forme de la caine:	 and this is the form of the cataracts:
des scrophules	Of scrofulous tumors

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	Of shoulder dislocation
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first address the dislocation initially.

aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	 Afterward allow the patient to rest, and do not move their limbs for long periods until they are well supported.

Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	 Because the joint is repositioned, and there may be bone fractures and the patient feels better.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	 When in the stomach there are coldness and excessive moisture affecting its temperament, causing numerous types of catarrh to occur, and following usual remedies it brings no benefit; then it is necessary for the patient to lie supine on their back, extending their legs and arms.

et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	 and the cauldrons should be placed as close to each other that they prick both legs on their knee, and the cauldrons should form according to this shape without crowding.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	 And if you see a large fire cautery within the stomach according to this form;

Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the treatment of the wound we have obtained before it is healed.

et c’est li forme:	 And here is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	 And if you wish to do so, fire these scalp wounds with cautery, if you are skilled in the art and careful not to burn the entire face as it would dry out all of the body.

Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	 When you have an abscess in the liver, and observe if it's on the surface of the liver or underneath its membrane.
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	 If it is on the surface, then the patient feels pain but not too severe;
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	 And if it's underneath, then they feel unbearable pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	 And when this treatment requires a mirror, the patient should be placed propped up on his bed;

aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Afterward, follow the treatment for pus removal until it is cleaned.
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	 And it does not require any other method of this cauterization than by those who have studied extensively in the art of medicine, and through whose hands these diseases have spread at some point.

dou cautere de pleuresin	Of the cauliflower-like swelling

et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	 And do not grip too tightly with your hand, but rather open widely as in smelling.

et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	 And then a great pain occurs, as we have said with abscesses of the liver.

de la mice	Removing hair from the area with fire cautery can cause burning and discomfort to the patient, but it may also lead to quicker healing if done properly under professional guidance.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When treating the disease known to us as 'mice' and its divisions in wounds, if there is no improvement, then there are three methods of fire cautery that all work well.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	 There is a method where you make three or four cauteries, aligning them according to the length of the vein, following the liver cautery that we have mentioned before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	 and do not hurry with your hand over all the cauteries, and let the patient lie on their back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	 And another method of cauterization is to heat the one with two horns, as we have shown in shoulder dislocation.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	 And lift the edge that is at the vein's location or where the patient'cuesthesis comes from the left side, and make elevations as you lift the edge according to its breadth, following the body's length, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	 After inserting two inflamed nerves until the core is pierced on the other side, then use a fire cautery, and so there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you see, causticize with all the cautery at three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After the cure when it has become swollen for long periods, this means moving as the other previously mentioned treatments.
de ydropisie	From dropsy (edema)
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Caustics are not used in hydrotherapy; that is called "ascluetae" method.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When you treat according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is time for you to make four cauterizations around the buttocks, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back above the spine, and one at the genitals;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 and place the caustications close to the esophagus near the core.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After leaving the cauterization open for long periods to drain pus, do not abandon treatment of the patient after caustication;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing would proceed swiftly, and they will be together with two intentions with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The form of the fire caustic for the abdomen is as we have previously shown.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 and that for the back be an olive-shaped piece, just as it has been set here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	From the swelling of the veins
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in one who is diabetic and full of golden-colored pus, it is necessary that you causticate on the back between the little finger and ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 and lift your hand with the caustic moving towards the tailbone.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not go too deep in, so it would draw out the yellowish sweat and be done with the caustic tool accordingly: according to this shape.
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After, do two caustics on each leg at the ankle joints.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 and let the caustic be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, on the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 And let the cauteries remain open for a long time to heal properly, so that they close completely.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 After treating other wounds as we have described.
de la menoison	Of a dislocation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When a solution of the stomach comes from cold and moistness, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and intestines have been weakened, they cannot be treated by conventional methods.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient is suffering greatly with strong virtues, then make a large fire cautery on the stamency as described above or an intestinal cautery, where the cautery circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and four subtle fires within all the fire of leeches are applied, and two on the groins.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moistures and the patient suffering, then perform fire cautery on the fingers, and one caustic point on each joint, and two small cauteries above the stomach near the large ones, because it is beneficial when there is good assistance for treatment.
de la cure des emorroydes	of treating swellings
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When bunions are at the base of one or more toes and are old and consist of large cold and damp corrupted humors, they should be treated as we have explained in sections; if it does not help, then do cauterizations.

et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 And if you believe the stomach is cooled and the flesh does not cook, and the face swells, then on the face apply a large cauterization to the stomach as previously mentioned, and another on the liver, and several small cauterizations in other areas;

de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage called "theal"

de plaie mal curee	of a wound improperly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening wounds, we will discuss this in detail; if there comes a disease that cannot be healed except by fire cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 When there is an occurrence of fistula and it becomes old and rotten with corrupted moisture, you should examine thoroughly the entire tent, and know its full extent.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After the caustic that appears hairy is set and inserted into the fistula according to the amount that was previously entered therein, continue with the caustic until the corrupt and rotten body parts are consumed, once, or twice, or thrice, depending on how much is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And watch for burning of nerves which are within, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the fistula reaches into the body of the bladder and intestines, watch for these lumps, do not attempt to cut them out in place without knowing whether they are benign.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After healing the lump as much as it becomes healthy, and if the lumps are swollen, and materials have been long extracted, then know that the lump is entirely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if materials have not been extracted, understand that the lump is inflamed, and corrupting the bone at its root.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And thus, as one of those which we say in place.

de la dolor dou dos	It causes great pain in the back.
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or from percussion, or from too much blood loss, or from resembling spread cold matter, of none of these matters does cautery hold value, except for those coming from an influx of cold substance.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 After the patient has been purged with foul pilules or other similar substances, they should be made to stand on their back where the pain is felt, three lines marked by dots, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 And let the cauterization be done according to the cauterizing method called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 and if you see, make III caturers or IIII at the central vertebra in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 This disease often comes to young children, and the signs of its onset are that their necks become tight when they move, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 and you find it in the lowest spine and it appears among the others above.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this wound and examine it, then cauterize with a caustic cautery as follows.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 If the fire cautery marks each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see, using a cutting caustic around the spine at points two or three lines apart, and they are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After healing the wound until it is clean as we have said, and be careful not to perform caustic treatment in a location full of nerve tissue.
de la dolor des jointes	For the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When joint pain is from moistures that are spread to every limb of the body, and when the pain comes in the foot, which physicians properly call "gout," and when it is due to cold causes and cannot be cured by medicines, then they are treated with caustics in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 Make the fire cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterizing be of an olive shape in this manner:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if there is a need to grasp above the face of the foot, then make caustic treatment everywhere that we call "none".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And when the pains reach to bones and other joints, which happens often, then make fire cautery on each big toe with three or four cauterizations from each part, for all olive-shaped caustics.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if more is needed, then make it more, but do not hold your hand away too far until the color of the skin has scorched.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains extend to the knee and back, treat with the fire cautery as we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if the pains are in the hands, make small indentations around the fingernails.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there is no pain in the fingers, make indentations on each joint and along the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 and if pains come near the edges or shoulders, caution each area, and give good care to the patient while administering remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you manage it well and purge moisture, he will be made whole with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	For the treatment of scurvy:
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When numbness comes to the fingers and they become limp with new symptoms, it is necessary when you see them healed, that you do not use any remedy on that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 and let him use things that ease his stomach so the puke rises from within.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 After he has sat on his back between your hands, command him to wash the area until it is restored, and reset the joints in your arms, and sew up from under the numbness around the bone of the thumb, and do a sign like three-quarters of a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Then heat the cautery of which this is the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until he is clean and his eyesight is clear.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then reset the bones to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 and ministers, you shall dress your hand so that they do not return backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and work well on the patient's thighs, and place a cord under him, then a strap over the thighs, and another over his foot where he feels pain in his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 then place the cautery on the mark with your entire hand, and keep it straight and as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat again until you get to the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 and be subtle that the flesh does not protrude when you perform the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 That you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 And so that the patient does not die or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that when you come up to the bone with the cautery, your works are of no value.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And it is necessary that the fire cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and large people also proportionate to their stature.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days he will treat the burn with butter until the scald is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After other salves are applied until it is healthy, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is well-healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary that its nourishments be lengthened so that the boils do not break out when he gets up to walk in his room.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after forty days, when he wishes to get up, let him be adorned with a well-made belt, and wear it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 And have good rest, that he works little and guards against excessive drinking of liquids and eating, and shouting too much.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when teaching this, be completely free from harm.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I will say hereafter the treatment of cutting within this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of abdominal surgery
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When windings come into other bellies and are known to you that they do not grow anymore, then make the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let it be one third of their size.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 Afterward, as we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 And none of the ancient ones have said that you should apply fire cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 But first mark the level of the head and draw a line for the width above the stone, and another one below, and place your hand throughout the entire fire scalpel.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 However, the first incision is lighter and easier to move.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	From old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or being struck, and this pain lasts a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective, then it should be cauterized with the fire scalpel known as "points", and the incision should be made according to the length of the member, its size, weakness, strength, location of twists, and pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 If it is free from harm with the first cauterization, it is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If such is the case, commence another cauterization upon it, as custom dictates that it should be moved to the limb closest to it, so it requires you to make the cauterizations until the patient is free from harm.
de meselerie	Medicinal treatment
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 Sometimes they are healed by fire for great help, and particularly the illnesses that come from the decay of moisture and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 Can you see it cauterized, take care if the disease is at the beginning, and if it is treated according to what we have said in the division, and neither recedes nor remains, and you suspect that corruption may affect the entire patient, then make V cauteries on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I am making V upon the forehead, and one near the end of the eyebrows.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 and III on the II horns, and I behind the temple area.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 and leave the hand to where the cautery reaches almost to the bone, and stay until blisters form so that vapors of large humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 and cauterize above the eye as it appears before you.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 If the messenger is scattered throughout;
