et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 And if it is clearly visible, then you must perform the cauterization with the cauterizations that we have mentioned previously: on the front of this area, and two near the neck, and six along the spine at the back, and one above the groin and another below, and two under the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 And two along the ribs, and two at the shins of the feet, and one on each joint of the hands and toes, and over the palms' hollows.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And beware of the nerves that lie behind the calves, do not cauterize them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 And never perform a cauterization on the bone of the wrist and one on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver's location.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that the more you perform cautery, the greater the aid it provides, and benefits accrue.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the patient feels no pain during cautery as healthy ones do, because their body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it should be that the cauterization is large or small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find in methods of handling iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing them with a paste made from flour several times with honey and other remedies until they are healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and poultices, and it is not healed, then you perform cautery on the limb according to its size and severity.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and let the cautery be slightly painful at first touch.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat with ointments until healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 And at no time is done cautery and to the hand, foot, or back, when it follows the nerve that moves the limb, thus this swelling occurs.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And in any case, no one interferes unless they are familiar with the limbs and the exit of the nerves moving within the body.
de albaras	In times past, there were certain individuals who could be found in various towns known as 'albaras', specializing in the treatment of wounds with their knowledge and skills.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease called "albaras" is old, and medical means are ineffective, then you should cauterize with a hot iron somewhat small, according to the quantity of blood seen, until it turns white and changes color.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 Then the treatment with fine flour and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood of calf's gallbladcuetts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And mix all together, bind with cloth, and apply heat to the area until it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a sore begins to develop, and you see it as an opportunity for treatment, use the fire cautery in the shape of a circle around the entire sore area.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 And yet the wise say to perform cautery just as with a gonorrhea.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 And yet it does not seem good to me, for I believe that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never wanted this to happen before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 A more proper course is that it should be cauterized nearby, with the cautery called "circulation," as we have said in many of cauldrations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the inflammation that cannot die down
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When some have an illness called "adubelati," and it delays death or due to the excessiveness of its effects or by the state of the patient when they are very old (that is to say, too weak) and have little blood, or for a while.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 And you see them hasten to die.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 Then, accordingly caulk around with many small burns by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	 After that, leave it as such.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see the entire cautery pierced, heat the cauldron of which there is a hole:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And put your hand in the midst of that illness called 'adubelati' until the cauldron feels its core, and be such cauldrons that the patient senses behind them somewhat so that the course of the pus is directed.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the treatment until it is completely healed perfectly.
li cure dou feu par fer	The healing of fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another way to name the disease is "corrodens," and it's nothing but a mass on the limb, as fire dries out logs in a similar manner.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this illness on site which can suffer fire caulking altogether, then fan the burns widely small and large as appropriate for its location or disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 After caulking all parts until you have removed all the infection and nothing remains of it, that everything which is corrupted be excised.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then let it be for three days, and apply poultices with oil until the burns from fire are healed, and all corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After applying the ointment treatment causing warmth.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days no health returns, this is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if not, then resume caulking on that which remains of the corrupted parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this inflammation is sometimes treated with cold medicines at the site of fire cautery.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 However, fire cautery is more helpful; and I have already described the treatment with cold medicines in the section on poultices.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 Take the quantity you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	small pearls coming to the fingers
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Many times it happens that under the feet is a disease we call "close," which is a large swelling affecting the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the fire treatment for this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 It is to know fire cautery and water hot cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Fire cautery is like heating an iron as with the blunt end of a bowl, and it should be made of good iron to accommodate the nail at all parts, and have subtle edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 After heating it thoroughly on the nail, turn your hand all around the nail until it feels hot at the point of the nurture.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 and leave it as such for three days until it begins to form pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 First make a poultice of mashed herbs with honey, and leave the poultice on throughout the night, and it will draw out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat the place of application with soothing ointment until it is healthy again.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if they are turned towards the rear of the body, and this often happens in hands and feet, it is necessary that you apply a hot water cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	 and occurs in one manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 take a bone of iron or lead, or a spatula blade, and place it on the nail and its root, that is to say for warts:
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 and place the bone so that it surrounds completely, then put some hot water on it, hold your hand firmly, and press your hand as you turn so that the edge of the bone reaches the root of the nail, allowing the hot water to reach deep down to the root:
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 The patient endures a bit of the tickling of hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 Then leave it so, and it will detach from all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 So do another afterward, until you have examined all those on the body; then treat with ointments that contain warmth.
li cure dou trembler	by tin la ouest anyt lesse s’enlde;
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 When anyone suffers from trembling due to coldness or fever of the quartan kind or other, it is necessary that you make four cauldrons on the spine of their back, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 and one near them, and one over the stomach at the olive oil caustic.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 If they will continue to tremble, it will preserve their health of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	Of purulent swellings
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Never appear visible in front of a body bathed or pus-filled lesions, which come from large corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 if in the first instance when you appear that you make cauldrons over each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 A subtle cautery made of mastic wood, where the tip is grasped by fire or a long-rooted astragalus, or with a lenticular caustic.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And at no time should they be cauterized from the start when noticed, according to this manner, and they cannot grow any lumps in front, but are relieved of excess which comes about, and become healthy.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 But it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery has been cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Many times there occur great bleedings from the artery that is severed at the wound that comes to the periphery, or in the incision of an abscess, or with a caustic on a limb, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 And it is a very difficult thing to stop bleeding.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 And in any case if this occurs with someone, quickly put your index finger on the wound of the vein, and strain it very hard until the bleeding subsides from under your finger, so that no more blood flows out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 then apply small to large olive oil-based fire caustics until they are all reddened.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 then take I (an unspecified medical substance), whether large or small depending on the wound and its location where the artery runs, and apply the fire caustic to that vein while holding your finger, until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps when you lift your thumb over the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And continue doing so one after another until the bleeding has stopped.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 Ensure you do not injure the nerve nearby, and that no other harm befalls the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 And know that if the vein cuts off, it cannot be properly tied again when the vessel is large; unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 or through cauterization, or by pulling out when it is not treated, or by strongly binding with thread, or by applying medicines that can stop the bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 and thus be tied off and strained accordingly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer proper stanching by wrapping tightly with cloths or applying burning substances above, or other similar things; if it does not help much.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if it happens to anyone and they do not have a scar or medicine present, you should place your index finger over the wound of the vein as we have said, and press firmly until it is tied off above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 And it should not move, but the cold sweat must often be very cold until the blood is congealed and thickened.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 Therefore make incisions forward as needed for cauterization and medicine application.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of wound treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about all illnesses that require fire-cauterization or burning medicines, as well as poultices and salves, along with their preparations and forms.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And I have included that chapter on head injuries up to the skull, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same method for what is found easier and as you wish.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	In starting this, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn in this chapter there is greater risk and fear than with the first of cauterizations, and therefore more caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incision on an abscess, and wound care, and arrow extraction, and cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 When there is doubt and fear, death comes to some.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I caution you to not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For there are many ways in which people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 If they come from such who are so afflicted with their illness that they die easily due to the severity and extent of their disease.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And one must have fear for these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And there are some who lose their senses, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "Wait," they claim, "I am healed;
et li maladie est despitouse.	 And the disease is treacherous.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 You should not easily consent to those who come to you in this manner, but rather put greater trust in your honor than in your desire, and do not act foolishly but judiciously based on what you are sure of and can have taken and lost.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 And use prediction and indication in treating your patients so that health may be restored.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 And this will help you to achieve good reputation, glory, and the memory of God.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	And I have ordered this treatise by sections as I spoke of the section on cauteries that I instructed from head to toe, so that you may find it more easily what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Full of water at the top
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 I say that this illness often occurs in infants during childbirth, and when the birth is too strenuous for the infant's head.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 and it never arises from any known cause.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 And I have never seen this disease occur in adults, and all those that I've seen it has quickly brought death.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 and therefore, it seems to me worthwhile to pay closer attention to this aspect of treatment.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I have seen a child whose head was swoln with water and the skull grew every day until it could no longer support itself.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 And due to so much moisture it caused death, and this moisture is gathered from under the bone above the shoulder blade, between the flesh and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And when such work is done if the moisture is between the flesh and the bone, and abscesses are small, you make a wide incision into the skull.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And it shall be of the same length as we, until the moisture subsides.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 and then you do this for the shape of the paralysis:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more severe, and the abscess is larger, make two incisions shaped like a cross as follows:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 And if the moisture is from under the bone, and the signs you see at the corners of the head are exposed on each side, and the sharp pain occurs when you press it with your hand inside, and this has not been restored to its place:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 If it is necessary, you must make three cuts within the head as follows:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 After the incision, remove all pus.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After making the incisions of linen and powders, add wine and oil, and leave it so until the fifth day.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then remove it, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, allowing the head to be evenly pulled out, and have the patient eat dried meat with a little moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another way of incising is to examine whether there are signs of large abscesses or collections of water.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 because it should never be present beforehand.
aucune fois derrier;	 and it should never be behind either.
aucune fois en destre;	 nor on the right side. 
et aucune fois en senestre.	 And never to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore cut where there is an abscess open, and fill with water, and heal according to what you are able.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 and be careful not to cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 and allow for a flow of blood, so that the patient may die from the loss of blood and evacuation of fluids.
de reume	Restore
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a disease called "catarra" occurs in the eyes or legs and the illness is longstanding, and medical treatment does not help, then the final remedy is the fire cautery where you cut two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 It is therefore necessary, when you see them covered, that the patient turn their head backward.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 then rub the wound with a rough cloth until you see the vessels, and then remove all bandages from the patient's neck.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 then look where it bleeds, and the veins on both sides are behind the ears, but few have been put back.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Then sign the edges of the wound with a heated piece of iron, then cover both sides with a thick bandage made from two parts until it reaches near the bone and is wide at the top.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see, insert the strip underneath the artery and cut above it as two parallel lines across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is opened, blood flows continuously upwards from it.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the artery does not open upon feeling, it is necessary that you measure the space of three fingers, then sign with a hot piece of iron and continue until reaching the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 and that amount of blood you must let flow is six ounces, and possibly a little more or less, depending on what the patient can tolerate, and the replenishment of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 if it remains under the bone with no spinal cord exposed, then apply a dressing where there are none, then bandage and treat with ointment until healed.
de emigrainne	Of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When migraine comes early with acute catarrh, due to moisture of tears and heat in the temples and old headaches and similar things, and it is treated by methods of medical remedies which do not benefit, so we draw out the arteries from the temples and perform cauterization as we have written.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 And the method of extracting them is such that the patient pulls back the hair from his temples and listens to the artery which opens in the temple, for it opens well by its pulsation, and is not easily replaced as with some men who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 and if it is restored, the patient should stretch their neck with a piece of cloth, then rub the area with an abrasive cloth, and apply warm water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 then take the splasmatil from where it is formed:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 then lightly scar the skin until you reach the artery, then cut it at the corners, and tie it off with threads from each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 And if the arrow is fine, pierce to the tip of the hook bone, then bind that part according to the quantity of two joints.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not properly set, then he will always have pain throughout all of it.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 And treat from six to three inches, just up to three inches.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 And if the arrow is large, it must be tied in two loops of strong, twisted silk thread to prevent decay at the wound site and ensure blood flow away from the wound.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then bind the excess tissue between the two loops at the same time, and then, if you see it necessary, cauterize with a surgical hot iron up to the bone as long as the joints are cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 This is the completed work; if the patient does not have a fever and is of warm temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 For the fire cautery serves to finish the pus:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 Because it is of greater aid in dealing with pus.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 Or, for extracting the artery, one should fill its place with old cotton and then put it back well made.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when you remove them, be sure to treat with dry medicines that produce heat and bandages until it is healthy.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if there is no blood flow as you do this, quickly cover it with fire cautery, where you fill its place with vitriol and stretch your hand that the wound be cleansed.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 And if you do not have it in sight, keep your hand on its place until the blood flow freezes, and apply cold water there until it flows again, and wrap as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And he who performs the extraction of arteries should causticate the vein with this sharp fire cautery in two parts, but the sharpness must be well tempered to preserve the heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when inflammation is too intense, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And it should be between the two knives with a space in the middle, and then when you have secured both blades, use the hot iron until reaching the bone, and cut the vein into two halves.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 and they should be separated between the two edges because it is not entirely reliable with this type of fire cautery in every case.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and here are the forms of the fire casters:
des larmes	From tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	 When the tears from the eyes descend into veins near the forehead's strength of flesh, and it does not benefit at all from medical treatment done there, and you see the face of the patient turn red, and feel their forehead tremble as if in fear.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	 And if they are held oily and damp so that the skin of the paper is chalky, and the papers are swollen, and scorched by the heat of tears, then this treatment may be necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	 And they called the old remedy "contusion treatment," and so you make it over to the patient with this condition on their forehead, then create three cuts or evenly spaced according to the length of the forehead.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	 and one of the cuts just like two thumbs together across the forehead down to the bridge of the nose, and the others two fingers above the skin, but beware not to incise the arteries that are at the level of the two fingers.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	 And align your hand with the extension of the two jawbones, so that each wound has a length equal to three fingers spanning the joints.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 And prepare a piece of sponge and several cloths for soaking up the blood, then use the spatula to apply it twice on each part where this shape is found.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	 From the incision that extends from the temple to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	 And scrape off all the core material that is between the two incisions across the entire facia overlying the bone; then make another opening from the middle incision to the other second one, and then extract this pus-like substance.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you place in the first cut an instrument called "culterellum," which is very sharp on one side and also smooth but not cutting on the other, and this is its form.
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	 And place the splint facing towards the chest near the heart, and the underside of the ribs towards the bone, and support it as much as it reaches to the middle opening.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	 And cut off all the vessels that arise from the head down to the eyes until the incision is continuous up to where it opens into the core; then make another opening in the middle incision up to the other one.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	 And then remove the blood evenly, and express its location for collecting the blood.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	 Then place a tent of fine cotton in each cut, and cover with cloths soaked in wine, oil, and herbs, ensuring no abscesses form.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And after three days, let the joint heal, and abundantly apply a water-based poultice, then treat with a balm of basil oil, along with other remedies used to heal wounds, until it is sound.
dou reume des eulz	To examine the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	 When anyone suffers from frequent and long-standing gout, and you see the eyes swollen and small, causing weakened vision, and burned corneas.
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	 When the hair falls out, causing intense pain at the crown, and the patient sneezes.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	 Then from these occurrences understand that such materials and those cataracts come only from many veins, and the physician treats accordingly if it is so.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	 And instruct the patient to place his forehead on it, then make a large cut in the middle of the forehead, and another with wide notches.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	 And begins with the cut of the left temple to the right temple, up until just before the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	 and remove your hand from the nerves near the temples that move during eating.
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	 and when the bone is exposed, draw all the blood onto an absorbent sponge, then between the two edges of the wound insert a piece of old cotton, attempting to stitch it with thread.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	 then place washed rags soaked in wine and oil on top, and beware of hot abscesses;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	 When it is fractured, you must rub the bone until a callus begins to form, then treat with things that are beneficial for healing, which should be done regularly.
En teil maniere:	 In such a manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	 Take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophonium, and mix them well.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	 And apply it to these wounds regularly to promote healing.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	And for the eaves by applying warmth from an ear and pouring thereof with oil or other liquids into the ear, and the beneficial properties they are found in the distillations; and then let it become so that li quidem.
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	 All that drips from the ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	 either grains, or animals, or stone fragments, or similar things made by man.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	 such as seeds that fall from the ground, beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	 or things that flow out like water and easily, similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	 When it is a stone in the ear or other matter not close to the ear, and does not grow within the ear, place the ear towards the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	 If you see a stone, and it drips any small amount of purple oil or sesame oil, then make an incision to extract.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	 And he makes the patient sneeze due to a condition, and blows his nose when sneezing occurs, placing cloth or woolen strips around the ears.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	 And extends the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	 Often comes as a result of this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	 And if it does not come to pass, the refined extraction is performed for which follows the method:;
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	 If it comes out with the fine probes, that's good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	 If not, then refined extraction is performed using a small double-ended hook.
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	 And if it still does not come out, then make a grape-sized incision and push the chief of the incision or an opening in the ear with force, and stuff soft wax around the incision so that nothing can enter through the incision.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	 Then treat with a strong fire, as often it comes this way as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	 And if it does not come in any particular way, then take pitch to which he applies feathers, and uses an instrument as needed for this purpose, placing some cotton around.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	 Then press the pitch on the stone or whatever it may be, and treat with a strong fire.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	 And if it does not go out from all the things we have said, then hasten to split the ear as soon as an abscess appears and pus emerges, and spasm occurs.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	 And the way of the split is that you first comfort the patient in his headache and then drain the blood according to its strength. Then make him sit between your hands, turning the ear upwards, making a small cut at the base or edge of the ear.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	 And it is to be torn as with the crescent moon, until you reach the stone, then push according to your strength, and suck in haste into your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And perform the healing until it is clean.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	 And if there are grains inside and they swell, then administer an extraction.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	 And if it cannot be expelled, then apply a small sucking cups (spatula) subtly according to this form: [Here should be the explanation of the method]
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	 and perform an incision at the site of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	 But do not attempt it when you think that the grain is softened by earwax moisture until you have tried many times.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	 Then extract it with subtle forceps and the suction cup, as we have said, so that the extractions may succeed.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	 Therefore if the grain gets into the ear, it is necessary for the patient to cough up phlegm first, and fill the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	 And let them rest on that same ear where the discharge is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	 If it falls out by itself, this is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	 If not so, take many small pieces as per the length of your string or ribbon and scald them in fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	 And put the patient's small pin or pincers in his ear, and draw out from it on one side with fingers from another piece of string.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	 And continue to do this until all the matter has been extracted piece by piece, and so it will be fully removed.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	 And if you see this, take a bamboo stick, and insert one end into the ear, and heat the other end in fire until it is properly charred.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	 Then make others as mentioned before, so that all has been extracted.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	 During the extraction of an animal, if it is a small creature like a flea or similar thing, treat it as we have said in the section on wound care.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	 But if it is of large size and can be felt, then make an incision for drainage.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	 And this is the easier thing to remove that may be in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	 In the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat them as we have said in the section on drainage and dealing with secretions, if the remedy does not help, it is necessary to examine the ear in sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	 If there are no worms, if the fine secretions are drained, and they do not appear, take this paste of which is made.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	 And it must be narrowed from below and widened above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	 And insert the finer tip into the ear according to the amount of pain suffered by the patient, then proceed directly to all parts.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	 Do this often as long as they are well rested.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	 And if they do not comply with exiting, then plug around the wound with cotton as I have instructed in the stone.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	 and if they do not exit as we have said, then administer infusions that the ancients have tested in arrow wound incision, and you will find them or treat with infusitions.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	 and if you distil your oils and medicines into the ear using this instrument, as shown here: [The following line would typically be accompanied by an illustration in a medical treatise from that time period]
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	 And [it is] made of silver or copper without small holes, and above openings for distillation.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	 And [to] press the essence during distillation with an adequately crafted copper instrument for this purpose, and if you see any residue, wrap it around the tip promptly with clean cloth.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	 Then pour in your oil or juice, and what you see of your medicine in the jar, and let it be placed in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	 Then put all the residue into the cloth and press with your hand quickly while the oil is still distilling or emerging from the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	 And let the patient smell it deeply, and be so that the distillation is slightly warmed by fire just as it is distilled in the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	 And keep it from being too cold, for the medicine would not be as effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	And for the eaves by applying warmth from an ear and pouring thereof with oil or other liquids into the ear, and the beneficial properties they are found in the distillations; and then let it become so that li quidem.
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	 No child is born without any eyebrows or ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	 and this same thing happens in individuals through a wound or a foreign object lodged inside the ear, and these blockages often do not extend fully into the ear canal if one cannot see them.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	 And it never happens that they lose their eyebrows completely, and what they see is fine.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	 Therefore, if it comes in but cannot be seen, it requires careful treatment and certain preparations, and when visible, one should place the affected ear towards the sun.
et regarde dedens:	 and examine inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 if you see an obvious obstruction, so that the work involves this spiral structure of which here is the shape:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	 And it is to pull and incise before and behind completely flat, so that it does not affect the ear.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	 If the obstruction is of a bone or body part of the ear, use delicate forceps and gently manipulate it until all pieces are removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	 And if there are obstructions in the ear, take a fine and gentle razor and warm it by fire, then place it on the edge of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	 If you feel the obstruction and the patient feels great pain in their hearing, pierce it lightly, and ensure that you do not strain the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	 Then place a tent in the ear according to its width on the perforation, and apply honey with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	 Do not do this until the wound is healed, then take a tent and apply honey with rosewater ointment, and powder with crushed cobalt.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 If you see an ear flying away, it is necessary to pierce the tent and move another bloody veil with a mold made of rose oil and wax until the swelling subsides.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat until it becomes healthy again.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, immerse a sponge and cover with cold water towel, place it on the ear, and apply other treatments that are used for treating blood by distillation.
de la char des papieres	From the papers of Char
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	 This bladder that arises from the hairs when they are wet and dry requires that you stretch them with tweezers and pincers, and cut off a small piece of their roots.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	 Then pour on white vitriol paste.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	 And if it does not come off, then cauterize with the fine lens-shaped cautery and afterwards apply heat to the incised area.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	 and do so many times until nothing remains of their roots.
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	 And when they are cauterized by fire, their roots are burnt and do not return.
de la gresle	From scurvy
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	 Many times come on the skin from the body things that appear gritty in their form and hardness, and so this illness is called "hailstorm," a collection of excessive moisture above and below the skin.
li ovraiges est telz:	 The treatments are as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	 Take care if "hailstorm" changes from one side and the other, for it is an easy thing to know.
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	 Make them then wider apart, then lightly peel each part, and bind with bandages, then wrap.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	 If you cannot cover it without piercing the skin a bit, nothing is harmed to the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 And if the tear is large, assemble it with a stitch, and care until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	 And if it's small, do not apply any pressure, for the ointments will restore it quickly and prevent scarring.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	 And if the splinter descends into the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper and extract it with tweezebrushes, hold and press from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	 And if the paper is pushed away by the incision, do not worry about it.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	 When great frost is removed, wash the wound with salted water and treat the area to heal as quickly as possible until the patient is well again.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat from the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	 Exanthema is a grease that appears on cloths and papers above, occurring mainly in children rather than adults, causing great discomfort to their eyes, leading them to have watery mornings, and they cannot look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	 And because of this they lie on their faces downward, sleeping with closed eyes and the dampness from their eyelids causing swelling and giving them an appearance covered by exanthema in the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	 And when you press on the place with your hands and feel the exiting between bones.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	 The manner of treatment is such that the patient places their head on a pillow.
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	 And then take a linen cloth, and make a tent in the shape of a circle according to the quantity that each part contains, then place it on top.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	 And press both sides with your hands so that the discharge is gathered within the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	 Then make a small incision with a sharp knife to release the fluid, and it should not be larger than the wound made on the vein.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	 And make an opening in front as much as you find discharge.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	 And in various cases, discharge comes from the incision, according to the shape of a piece of white fatty tissue.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	 Remove it altogether with a whole piece of spotted cloth between your thumb and index finger, and turn your hand to the right and left until scattered.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	 And ensure that you do not insert it into the tear, that you do not widen the entire swath until the end, and do not break it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	 And if the sinew does not protrude at the beginning of the tear, then gently push the tear until it appears.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	 Then extract as we have said, then wet rags and water, and put under the sore, and bind with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	 And if it is for men who grind salt and apply it to spoil that moisture which has remained.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then the treatment should be continued until healed.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if it comes to a hot abscess at the place, then treat with plasters soothing until healed.
des poilz des papieres	From the hairs of parchment papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	 When hairs grow in paper other than their nature, and are aged, they harm the eyes, and bring about ways of diseases such as accustomed tears and softening of the papers and scurf, until it is caused by the destruction of the eyes.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	 And there are four methods of treatment:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	 or by fire caustic alone, or by medicinal ague as instructed in this chapter on fire cautery, and is done either through incision and suturing or with lancets, as I will describe.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	 It must be that you place the patient's head in your lap, then turn the paper of oil to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	 if it is so positioned, this is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	 if not, then place a needle all the way through with thread.
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	 and if it is near the edge of the paper or hair grows from there, draw the thread through to all sides of the paper and turn it as smoothly.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	 Then make at the part below the paper, below the hairs nearest to it, covering all around, from the great forehead down to the small.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	 Then extract the thread, and place under the paper a small tent of cotton and cloth, then gently press down on the paper with a molding form as a reed basket, and it is necessary that the shape be according to the quantity you see raised in the paper which is desired for all.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	 And if there is an area that requires cutting off a large quantity of paper as it has softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	 then make throughout the entire surrounding areas marked by you, and begin from the great forehead down to small.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	 And there is a split near the natural hair growth of a root, then insert the needle into one of its two corners, and scrape it thoroughly.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	 Then stitch the two lips with a thread made from fine wool using one needle, and let out blood, remove excess threads around both eyelids without any sticky substances, if you do this.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	 And if not, leave the stitching and threads for three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	 Then treat the wound without dry or constricting things, as the paper relieves at the discomfort of the wound and its healing, but stitches are moved (as ancient texts say), and this is a work without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	 And if by another method:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	 And it is that you shape the paper into a form similar to the willow leaf, as we have described before, at three inches in size according to the following pattern.
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then apply the force.
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	 And if you cannot hold the tongs, and the piece is not uniform, then take a needle with one thread, and wrap it around the form.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	 And add another thread near the large end, and the second thread near the small end, and interweave between them both threads evenly.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then lift your hand evenly and remove all the skin over which you have shaped, as we have described before, then stitch together the two edges of the wound with a seam, and care for it until it heals.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	 If an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with cerote and similar soothing ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	 And sometimes it happens that the hair of the paper is turned into:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	 If it becomes necessary to use what we have said about the incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	 But the stitching on either side is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	 The treatment of wounds follows this method:

de la racine des dens	From the root of the spine
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the roots remain during extraction, it is proper that you place cotton soaked in oil on the wound for one or two days until the area is smoothed over, then insert the instruments called "algofri," which make the head of the shoulder appear as if a bird's beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 And made hollow as a file, and it is shaped thus:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not pass through all these pins, it is necessary to expose the entire bone around the root and insert an instrument called "althali" (a splint), which resembles a staff:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 And be thick enough so that it does not break, and if the root sprouts from this place, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If not, assist with all possible means by which shapes can come hereafter:

et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools in front of him for teeth, and from this instrument that looks like large pincers, the form it takes is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 And these supports must be strong so that they cannot break, and know there are many of dense support.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 And likewise other supports, which are not counted:
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 And the wise master subtly uses his instrument by himself according to his practices and the diseases he demonstrates, because there are partial ailments or ancient teachings did not show instruments for variety of causes; so it does not break at all on the cart or other bones, or elsewhere where it protrudes. Seek the supports that should be used as I have told you, and assist with gestures such that this shape occurs:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 And they are large and well held to hold the bone, that it does not escape, but can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 And then restore it to its place with suitable remedies for this, and if there is decay in the bone, and it is small, that the patient has all this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 When the visible teeth do not follow the natural course of the body, and their shape is unattractive, especially in maidens, it must be known if the tooth root has been removed after the tooth, and it is not naturally placed on the right side, and cannot be pulled or filed down.
adonques lou raie;	 Then cut off;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 And if it is adhered with the tooth, take this instrument of which here is the shape, and it resembles a small beak, and is made of iron inwardly sharpened.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	Et place the coping piece by piece over time due to the hardness of the tooth, and because you do not move the others, and if it is apparent that one can be filed down, then file the coping so that its shape resembles this.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 And it is as with the limb of which needles are made;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 and in a similar manner to the bone from which nails are formed, and it is gently wound up little by little over several days so that it does not move until it sets.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 then the surface is completely smoothed at the end without any roughness, and if its density is too severe and it blunts the tongue, then you must file the sharp edges so that they are even, ensuring that it neither blunts the tongue nor corrupts speech.
quant li dent lochent	Whenever the tooth chips
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the tooth is loosened either by impact or falling out, and the patient cannot apply pressure under what they bite that it does not fall out, and you have treated them with constricting medicines but this is ineffective.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 If necessary, constrain with a thread of gold, for silver threads turn green and rust, but gold does not move ever.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And let the thread be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the quantity of space between the points.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you see the points aligned, take the thread and loop it twice between the two healthy points, then place the knot between the points until you reach another healthy point on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 Then resume coverage up to the part where you began, and gently yet skillfully pull your hand back until it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 And keep the ligature close to the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then wrap the head of the bone with iron wire using pliers, and join them, and position them so they do not touch the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 And then let it remain tight as long as possible, and if it loosens or the wires break, restrain them with another wire.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 If it remains and functions in this manner throughout its strength, and it is the form of the jawbones and the alignment of the two healthy teeth and the two replacements as you see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when a tooth falls out, reset it back in its place, freshly each time, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 And do not involve anyone who is wise and compassionate, nor at any time shape it as a tooth from an ox bone, but place it where the deficiency is, restrain it as we have said, and it will last and serve for long periods.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	:  And so, they should be ong-pie if the w such that heal;
