Si reis devant de grant raseurs, et aprés de plus subtilz, et ne cesser de ceu faire tant k’il soit bien.	If you have many coarse razors and finer ones after that, continue doing so until it is well done.
En chescune des autres tailleures capillaires et brisure subtil, covient que tu amenistres cause selonc son adrecement;	 In each of these hair-cutting techniques and subtle fractures, it is necessary to treat according to its specific condition.
et c’est chose que n’est mie reponue a celui qui a mis son estude en cest art.	 And this is something that cannot be taught to those who have not devoted their study to this art.
Et se li syfac est descovers, si covient que tu preignes I drapeil de lin, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et le moille en oile roset, et le mete sus la plaie;	 And if the sinew is exposed, it is necessary to take a bandage of lin cloth according to the amount of wound, and soak in oil rose water, and apply over the wound.
puis pren I autre drapeil doublé en II ou en III, et le moille en vin et en oile roset, et le met sus le premier drapeil;	 Then take another cloth doubled over two or three times, and moisten with wine and oil, and place it on the first cloth.
et fai ceu plus legierement que tu pues, que tu ne grever lou syfac, puis aministre par desus I autre liien, et ne l’estraindre mie fuer que tant k’il teigne la plaie soulement;	 And do so more gently as you can, not burdening the patient's neck, then administer underneath it the ligature, and only tighten enough to just cover the wound.
et le laisse ensi I jor ou II, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, puis le deslie, et i aministre medicines si com racines de lis, et farine de veces, et poudre d’encens, et aristologe, et semblans choses;	 And leave it thus for one or two days until the abscess is soothed, then remove it, and apply medicines as with lily roots, and barley flour, and incense powder, and aristolochia, and such things.
et de ces choses fai poudre, et met sus la plaie, et i aministre adés medicines mondefians sens mordication;	 And make a powder from these things, and place on the wound, then apply remedies without biting.
et warde que li plaie soit adés nette, que tu n’i laissier mie l’oignement, ne n’i laissier mie assembler bowe, car quant bowe s’asemble sus la toile dou cerveil, si la corront et porrist, et avient au malaide grans malice;	 Ensure the wound remains clean and do not leave any pus or allow it to fester with bowels, for when bowels gather on the brain's cloth, they cause harm and great distress.
car quant on met sus lou syfac chose mordant, si nercist par desus.	 Because if one places something sharp upon a wound, it must be cauterized above.
Pren warde donques, se nulz mavais accidens vient au malaide, si com nos avons dit, si est doutable sens doute.	Therefore be cautious; if by chance something happens to the patient as we have said, it is uncertain and without doubt.
Et se noiror n’i vient fuers que por la medicine c’on a mise sus, que teil vertu ait, si covient que tu preignes une partie de miel, et III parties d’oile roset et en glue I drapel, et lou met sus lou syfac;	 And if darkness does not occur from the medicine applied, ensure it has potency; then you must take a piece of honey and mix three parts with rosy oil and one part woolen cloth, and apply it to the wound.
puis lou cure de manieres de cures qu’il couvient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then proceed with appropriate treatment methods until healed.
Saiches que aucune fois sont brisies les II parties dou neis desus, ou li une par li soulement, car ce sont II os;	 Remember that no time should the two parts of the neck above be broken or twisted, for these are two bones;
et cil desoz est cartillaginous, et ne brise mie, si ne fait fuer k’enbower ou tordre, et puis saine.	 And those which are dislocated are cartilaginous, and do not break or cause entrapment or twisting, and then they heal.
Et se l’une des II parties est brisie, si covient que tu boutes ton petit doi ou pertus dou neis, et met igal cele brisure dedens a ton doi indice, et au pouchet par defuer, tant que li neis reveigne selonc sa figure natureil;	 And if one of the two parts is broken, you must push your small finger or thumbnail into it, making an equal break inside the index finger joint, and along the hinge backwards until the nail regains its natural shape.
et fai ce legierement, et warde que li malaides ne sente dolor par ton ovraige.	 And do this gently, so that the patient does not feel pain from your action.
Et se li brisure est en la partie desus lou neis, et ne puet venir li dois au leu, si couvient que tu lou mettes igal au chief d’un rait un poc gros.	And if the fracture is in the part above the knee and cannot bring the foot to its place, it should be set level with a thin stick slightly thicker than usual.
Et se li brisure est de II pars, si refai autretel, et te haste de restorer lou premier jor, se tu pues;	 And if it is a break of two parts, do likewise and hasten to restore the first day, if you know how.
se ce non, aprés lou septime ou le disime, quant li apostemes chaus est apaisiez, puis bouthe au chief dou neis tentes de drapelz de lin, se li brisure est en une partie.	 If not, after the seventh or next day, when the swelling of the puncture has calmed down, then push at the tip of the nail with a fine linen cloth if the break is in one part.
Ou tu boutes I autre d’autre part, se li brisure i est;	 When you bind another from the other side, if there is a breakage there.
et soient les tentes si grosses qu’eles emplissent les pertus dou neis.	 And they are tented so large that they fill the windows with their presence.
Et dirent aucun restorour c’on doit moillier les tentes em burre, et muer chescun jor.	 And some healers say you must grind down the stings with butter, and change each day.
Il ne me semble mie que ce soit bien, mais covient qu’elles soient moillies en confection d’aubun d’uef, et de poudre de molin;	 It does not seem to me entirely good, but it is necessary that they be made of wool and egg whites, and powdered mill.
puis laisse la tente, tant que li os soit fers, et li cartilaiges endurcis.	 Then leave the tent, as long as the bone is hardened, and the cartilage stiffened.
Et aucune fois boute on ou neis pennes d’oie en leu de tentes, et si a I souef drapeil entor, et se tient la briseure, et soffle li malaides parmi;	 And never blow into the nose or eyes near these tents, and if there is a small vein present, and it holds the breakage, and blows on the patient's pain.
or fai lou kel ke tu vues.	 Or do whatever you see fit.
Et se apostemes chaus vient au neis tandis com tu i oevres, si i met cerote ou coton moilliet en oile roset, ou en .i. poc de dyaquilon.	When an abscess occurs near the eye as you work on it, place beeswax or cotton soaked in rose oil, or a drop of diaperin.
Et se apostemes chaus n’i vient, si met emplastre par defuer, de farine de sisament, et de poudre d’encens, confites avec aubun d’uef, puis met sus estoupes legieres, et ne liier mie lou neis;	 And if there are no abscesses forming, then apply plaster afterwards using fine flour, and powdered incense, mixed with egg whites, then place light gauze on it, but do not tie the nose or eyes.
et se li brisure dou neis est petite, et il est brisiés em menues pieces, si l’estrai as estrumens covenables a ceu, puis cout la fendure, et la cure de choses enjanrans char, et soudant, si com emplastres et oignemens covenables a ceu;	 If the break of the nose is small and it is broken into tiny pieces, then extract with suitable tissues, then cut the fracture, and treat various complex wounds and injuries, as appropriate poultices and ointments for this.
et s’il n’a dedens lou neis nule plaie, si lou cure de tentes, et i met cainnes de plonc, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If there is no wound on the nose and it has been treated with bandages, apply pledgets soaked in liquid until healed.
de la routure de la mandibule	For dislocation of the jawbone.
Quant li mandibule est route desoz, et il n’i a point de plaie defuer, et li brisure est defuer tant soulement, et n’est mie brisiez en dous, fuer que corbelz dedens, si le conoist on legierement.	When the jawbone is dislocated and there are no wounds nearby, and the fractures are minimal, so that it's not broken in two, but rather splintered within, if one can notice this lightly.
Il covient, se li brisure est en la destre partie, que tu boutes ton doi indice en la bouche dou malaide;	 It is necessary, if the breakage is on the right side, to insert your index finger into the mouth of the patient.
et se li brisure est en la mandibule senestre, si boute ton doi indice de la main destre, et boute la brisure dedens legierement, et l’afaite a l’autre main par defuer, et met igal.	 And if the breakage is on the left jawbone, insert your index finger from your right hand into it and gently press the fracture back in place with that hand, while supporting with the other hand evenly.
Et se li brisure de la mandibule est desevree en .ij., si covient que tu aministres extension de .ij. pars, tant qu’il soit igalz.	And if the fracture of the jawbone is displaced on two sides, it is necessary to arrange for an equal extension on both parts.
Et se commovemens des dens avient, ou routure, si les estrain d’un fil d’or ou d’argent ou de soie, puis met sus la mandibule brisie cerote, et met sus I drapel double;	 If movements of the teeth occur, or grinding, then tie them with a thread of gold or silver or silk, and place on a broken jaw cerate, and place under a double cloth.
et met sus lou drapel une grant estele bien faite, ou une piece de cuir igal, longe et large selonc la mandibule, et la lie sus au mues que tu pues, et comande a malaide qu’il se repose, et menjuce viandes legieres.	 And place the great splint well made upon it, or a piece of leather equal in length and width to the jaw, and tie it under the movements you can see, and instruct the patient to rest, and serve light meats.
Et se tu vois que li figure se chainge, si le deslie au tier jor, et puis remet a point ceu que c’est chaingiet;	 And if you see that the shape changes, then reset it every day, and then put back what has changed.
et met emplaustre sus, de la poudre dou moulin avec abun d’uef ou farine de sisament, aprés ceu que tu as osteit lou cerote;	 And place poultice on it, with fine-ground powder or meal flour from sesame seeds, after you have removed the cerate.
et met sus l’emplaustre lainne legiere, et se li emplaustres s’aert, et li disposition dou malaide ne se chainge, laisse le tant k’il soit sanez;	 And place a light bandage over the cast, and if the cast swells, and the patient's position does not change, leave it until healed.
maintes fois est sanez en III semainnes.	 Many times is healed in three weeks.
Et se apostemes chaus vient, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit maintes fois.	And if an abscess comes, arrange as we have said many times before.
Et s’il i a brisure et plaie ensamble, rewarde se nule piece de l’os en est ostee;	 And if there is a fracture and wound together, be sure no part of the bone has broken through;
si subtilie de l’oster as estrumens covenaubles a ceu.	 If subtly into the flesh near it.
Et se li plaie est estroite, si l’eslarge a flaime selonc ta necessiteit.	And if the wound is narrow, enlarge it as necessary according to your discretion.
Et quant tu avras ostees toutes ces pieces, et il n’i demore nule, si cout la plaie, s’ele est large, et met sus .i. des emplaustres covenaubles a ceu, por enjanrer char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	When you have set all the bones in place and they do not move out of position, if the wound is wide, cover with one or two bandages to support healing until it has fully mended.
de la forcele	To strengthen and fortify.
Li forcele brise plusors fois devant, devers l’espaule, et li brisure si est selonc III manieres:	 The severe fractures many times before, toward the shoulder, and the fractures are as follows in three ways:
ou elle est brisie et desevree en II, et i a pieces, et est li plus legiere a restorer;	 or it is broken and displaced into two parts, and there are fragments, and it is easier to restore;
ou il i a brisure avec plaie.	 or there is fracture with wound.
Et li ovraiges si est quant li brisure est sens plaie, que tu aies II ministres, si que li uns teigne l’ajutoire que sent la forcele brisie;	 And such works are when there is broken bone without wound, so have two assistants, one to treat the dislocated shoulder that feels weakened.
et li autres estende lou col vers la partie;	 and the other stretches the neck towards the injured area.
puis met igal la brisure a tes dois, si que li forme soit si com il covient, et n’i ait ne apparance ne chevement.	 then set the fracture with your hands, so that it forms as it should, and there is neither visible deformity nor instability.
Et se tu a mestier de plus estendre, si met desoz l’espaule au malaide une spere reonde de drap, ou de lainne, et soit grosse selonc ta necessiteit;	 And if you need to extend further, place a round rod of cloth or leather under the patient's shoulder as needed, and make it thick according to necessity.
et estent et lieve la forcele, et estraint le spere a ta main, si que tu mettes igal la brisure, si com il covient.	 and elevate and relieve the limb, holding the rod in your hand to ensure the fracture is aligned as it should be.
Et se tu ne pues traire le chief de la forcele au defuer, por ceu qu’elle vient em parfont, si covient que li malaides gise sovin sus son hatereil, et met desoz l’espaule .i. oreillier moien, et boute li ministres l’espaule aval, tant que li os de la forcele soit levez.	And if you cannot pull the head of the fractured limb towards the back because it comes out frontwards, then it is necessary for the patient to lie on their stomach, and place half an earthenware pot under the shoulder, with the assistants lifting the shoulder while keeping pressure until the bone in the fractured limb rises.
Et puis adrece la brisure a tes dois, et se tu lou trueves debrisiet, si covient que tu fendes sus;	 And then bring the fracture towards your hands, and if you find fragments, cut beneath them as needed.
et trai fuer les pieces legierement, et se li os ne puet joindre por aucun sormontement, si le cope a l’un des incisoires que tu as;	 And pull gently on the fragments if the bone cannot be joined by any splinting; and wrap with one of the bandages that you have.
mais que tu mettes desoz la forcele cest estrument, por warder lou syfac:	 but use a tourniquet for this instrument to prevent bleeding:
et semble une cuiller, et n’est mie chevez, et soit ausi large com il lou covient, selonc la grandor de l’os et la possance de l’uevre;	 and make it into a cup shape, not pointed, and be as wide as necessary according to the size of the bone and the strength of the hand:
et ait II chiés, si com tu vois, et soit li uns larges, et li autres estrois, si com est li routure de la plaie que tu as fait quant tu as trait les os;	 and have two handles, as you see fit, one wide and the other narrow, corresponding to the shape of the wound you created when setting the bones:
et quant tu es asseurez d’aposteme chaut, si cout la plaie, et se li routure est petite, ou tu doutes aposteme chaut, si emple la plaie de drapelz et de tentes, selonc sa quantiteit.	 and when you are sure of a hot abscess, cut the wound, and if the shape is small or you doubt it being hot, use a bandage and gauze as needed according to its quantity:
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si moille .i. drapel en oile roset et en aisil et en vin, et met sus.	When abscesses occur there, apply a cloth soaked in oil with roselle and spices, and place it on top.
Li estrignement de l’os, quant il est sens plaies et sens tailleure, est que tu mettes sus l’os l’enplaustre de la poudre dou molin et d’aubun d’uef, et met estoupes legieres sus, et met une spere desoz l’assele, se tu en as mestier;	 When the breaking of a bone is sensed with wounds and splinters, place plaster powder from finely ground mill on it, add egg yolk, and apply light gauze pieces over, and put a stick underneath the bandage if needed.
puis pren une tres grant bende d’une palme de large, puis met I drapeil double sus estoupes, et l’emplaustre;	 Then take a very wide strip measuring one palm in width, then put on two layers of bandages above the gauze and plaster.
puis pren une estele subtil de III dois de large et de lonc, et l’envoloupe entor celui bendeil, si que li chief dou bendeil soient pendant;	 Then take a subtle stick measuring three fingers in width and length, and wrap the entire bandage around it, ensuring that the top of the bandage remains taut.
et met l’estele sus la briseure, et torne le bendeil sus lou col, et desoz l’asselle sainne, et desoz l’asselle malaide;	 And place the stick over the fracture, then turn the bandage at the shoulder, and under a healthy lower joint, and under an injured lower joint.
et la ramoinne de chescune partie, et quant tu vois ke li lieure tient la briseure avenanment, et tu vois clerement que li estele ne se muet desus l’os brisiet, si le rewarde chescun jor, et quant li liiens eslaiche, si lou restraint;	 And the reset of each part, and when you see that the joint holds the fracture immediately, and you clearly see that the splinter does not move over the broken bone, then reward each day, and when the ligaments are relaxed, hold it in place.
et fai gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li met quant il dort I petit orillier desoz l’assele, por lever l’ajutoire en haut;	 And make the patient lie on their back, and put a small pillow under their shoulder to lift the dislocated joint upward.
si aligera li brisure de la forcele par l’aligement de l’espaule, ou tu li lie lou bras au col, et ne lou desliier se malvais accidens n’i vient, jusc’a XX jors;	 If you lighten the strain of the fracture by aligning the shoulder or tying the arm to the neck, and that it does not come off improperly until twenty days.
puis rencomence l’emplaustre, se tu vois qu’il en ait mestier, et l’estraint et le laisse ensi, tant qu’il soit restorez;	 Then resume the splint if it is needed, and hold and leave it so until it is restored.
et elle est restoree au plus en XXVIII jors, et en moins a aucuns homes.	 And it is restored within at most 28 days, and sooner for some men.
de la brisure de l’espaule	Of a shoulder fracture
Poc avient que li espaule brise ou large leu ne em mileu, et ne lou seit on fuers que par lou touchement;	 Occasionally the shoulder breaks or dislocates out of place, and it cannot be moved except by touching it.
si l’apareille selonc la figure de la brisure, et la ramoinne selonc sa forme natureil, en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	 if you set the fracture according to its pattern, and reset the limb in all ways that you can.
puis met sor le leu poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, et estoupes legieres, et met sus I drapeil double;	 then apply powdered lime with plenty of egg whites on it, and lay a light gauze over it.
puis met sus une estele large et subtil, un poc plus large de l’espaule, et se desoz l’estele est chevemens en aucun leu de l’espaule, si emple celle cheveure d’estoupes de lin, si que li estele siece igalment;	 then place a wide and fine bandage that is slightly wider than the shoulder, and if from the bandage there are gaps anywhere in the shoulder area, fill those spaces with lime starch.
et puis l’estraint a tout une grant bende fermement, si que li estele ne se mueve de son leu, et regarde le liien chescun jor;	 And then strain it firmly for a long while so that it does not move from its place, and monitor the ligaments each day.
et toutes les fois k’il amolist, si l’estraint, et met igal l’estele s’elle est fuer de son leu, et gise li malaides sus son costeit;	 And every time it swells, strain and make the bone equal if it is out of its place, and lift the patient on their side.
et li espaule est restouree en XX jors ou en XXV.	 And the shoulder may be restored in 20 days or 25.
Et quant cist nombres est acomplis, si le deslie, et soies seur, car ce n’est mie os qui se mette fuer legierement.	 And when this number is fulfilled, release it gently and support it, for it is not the bone that repositions itself lightly.
Et se une piece de l’os tent avant, et point desoz lou keur, si fent sus, et l’oste, et fai ceu que nos avons dit en la brisure de la forcele d’apaisier aposteme chaut.	And if a piece of bone protrudes but not from the skin, and it becomes swolebed, and there is inflammation, then follow what we have said in the treatment for an abscess to relieve discomfort quickly.
de la brisure dou pis	Of the fracture of the thigh bone
Li peis est aucune fois brisiez em mileu, mais ce avient poc;	 The flesh is never torn apart entirely, but this happens rarely;
mais il brise sovent au defuer.	 but it often breaks at the end.
Et quant il est brisiez emmi, si decline au desoz, et sent li malaides grant dolor, et faute d’alainne, et toust, et par aventure vomist sanc, et apert li chevemens en l’os brisiés, et lou sent om bien.	 And when it is broken inside, if it leans to one side, the patient feels great pain, weakness, heat, and perhaps vomits blood, with fractures in the bones that have been shattered, and he feels very ill.
Et li restoracion si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, et li met I cussin entre les espaules, puis presse les espaules, et li assemble les costes des II costelz a tes mains, et subtilie dou mettre igal a toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que li figure de l’os soit si com il covient;	 And the restoration is such that the patient lies on their back, and you place I cushions between the shoulders, then press the shoulders together, and articulate the ribs with your hands using II methods as possible until the shape of the bone is correct.
puis met sus emplaustres et estoupes desus l’estele subtil de salz, ou d’autre fust legier, et l’envoloupe en I drapeil, et la lie sus l’os brisiet, si qu’elle ne se mueve;	 Then place splints and plugs over the subtle bone of salt, or any other light material, and wrap it in a bandage so that nothing moves against the broken bone.
et torne le liien reondement au dos, et l’estraint avenanment, et rewarde chescune houre la liure, et s’elle ramolist, si l’estraint;	 and turn the ligature round to the back, adjust for comfort, and reward each hour of rest, and if it loosens, then tighten again.
et s’il lou covient desliier, por corrosion ou por prurite que vient au leu, ou dolor ou aposteme, si te haste, et lou deslie, et raie l’emplaustre, et adresce ceu qui i est venus de manieres de cures;	 and if it needs to be loosened due to corrosion or pruritus at the site, or pain or an abscess arises quickly, then untie it, remove the splint, and address whoever has come with methods of healing.
puis ramoinne l’emplaustre, et l’estraint tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then replace the splint and tighten as necessary to ensure stability.
de la brisure des costes	For a broken rib fracture
Saiches que li briseure des costes ne vient fuer que en leus gros aprés le dos, et au chief dedens, et ne ploient fuer que por ceu qu’eles sont glairouses;	 Acknowledge that rib fractures occur mainly on the outside after the back and within at the top, and they do not bend easily because they are brittle.
et le sent om bien a l’inquisition as dois.	 And it feels well to the touch near the joints of the arms.
Et li restoremens si est que tu met igal la brisure, si com il covient.	 And the mending is such that you make the break equal as it should be.
Et puis met l’emplaustre, et l’estraint d’une estele, se tu en as mestier.	 And then apply a cast, and use a splint if necessary.
Et se li brisure des costes est declinans au dedens, si sent li malaides tres grant dolor, et pointure, ausi com de pleuresin, car li os point la toile;	 And if rib fractures are descending inside, the patient feels intense pain and numbness, much like with suffocation, because the bone is exposed.
et alaine a poinnes, et toust et vomist grant planteit de sanc, et c’est de grief santeit, et li ancien i ont mis grant engien.	 and there are lumps, swelling, and excessive bleeding of blood, which is serious illness, and the ancients have applied significant remedies.
Et si a de ces qui dient qu’il le covient aministrer viandes qui enflent le ventre, por bouter la briseure au defuer.	And some say it is proper to administer meats that inflate the belly, in order to push out the breach.
Nos ne faisons mie ceu, que apostemes chaulz n’i viegne, s’il n’i est venus.	We do not make it so that abscesses are formed within if they have not come already.
Et s’il i est venus, si le saine.	If it has occurred there, if the joint is healed.
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on met ventouses sor le leu, por sucier forment, et c’est semblant a raison;	 And some say that one should apply cups on the outside to draw out fluids, and this seems reasonable;
toutevoie, doutance i a que li ventouse n’atraie les superfluitez au leu por la disposition de foiblece.	 Nevertheless, there is doubt as to whether the bladder draws excess fluids to that place due to weakness in its positioning.
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on doit covrir le leu de lainne moillie en oile chaut, et met on tentes entre les costes por metre igal la lieure entor, puis soit curez de la cure de pleurisin, de viande et de medicine.	And they say of these that one should cover the area with moist linen soaked in hot oil and place tents between the ribs to achieve equal pressure all around; then treat it with the treatment for pleurisy, flesh, and medicines.
Et se li malaides sent grant dolor qu’il ne puet soffrir par l’os qui point la toile, et doutance est au malaide, si covient fendre sus lou leu de la coste brisie, et covient mettre desoz I estrument por warder lou syfac;	 And if the patient feels great pain that they cannot bear from a bone protruding through the skin, and doubt occurs to them, then it is necessary to cut near where the broken rib is located, and it is appropriate to place an instrument there for protection.
et adonques doit on trenchier l’os, et traire legierement, et puis coudre les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, et le curez d’emplaustres, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then one must cut the bone, and gently pull it slightly, and then sew the edges of the wound if they are large, and treat with emplasters until healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient, si met sus drapelz moilliez en oile roset, et met sus lou leu;	 And if an abscess comes forth, then place a cloth soaked in rose oil on it and over the wound;
et cure tandis le leu de ceu qu’il covient a aposteme, et soit gisans sovins sus lou costeit ou il doit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And care while the location is such that it requires an incision, and let them lie on their side with support under the spine where they should be stable.
de la brisure dou col	From the break of the neck
Aucune fois vient briseure as os dou col, et poc avient k’il ploie;	 Never comes a fracture of the hip bone, and rarely does it bow.
et ausi a l’espinee dou dos.	 and similarly to the spinal column of the back.
Et quant ce avient a aucun, et tu vues savoir s’il sera sanez ou non, si pren warde se tu vois ses mains mollifiies et enflees et mortes, et ne les puet movoir ne estendre, et quant tu les poins d’une aguille, si ne lou sent.	 And when this happens to anyone, and you want to know if it will heal or not, watch carefully if you see his hands softened and swollen and dead, and cannot move them nor extend them, and when pricked with a needle, do not feel them.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz em plusors dispositions, et s’il les muet et sent bien quant on les estraint et point, saiches que li jointure de l’os est sauve, et que li malaides iert curez, s’on i met cure.	 Say that they are dead in various positions, and if you move them and they feel well when restrained but not moved, know that the bone's joint is preserved, and the patient will be healed if treated accordingly.
Et se semblans chose vient a l’espinee dou dos, et tu vues savoir s’il iert sanez ou non, si pren warde se li piez sont amollis, et se li accident i sont qui sont em mains, et sus lou dos saut ventositeit et egestion sens volonteit;	 And if similar things occur in the spinal column of the back, and you see to know whether it is stable or not, take care if the feet are softened, and if there are accidents that have taken place, and on the back swells with windiness and egestion without will.
et quant on l’a sovineit sus son ventre, si saut egestion sens volonteit.	 And when it has swollen above its belly, if there is egression without will.
Et quant il est sovinez sus son dos et il vuet asseller, si ne puet.	 And when it has been soved on its back and it wants to sit up, it cannot.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz:	 Know that they are deadly.
si ne laboreir mie en sa cure.	 If one does not labor at their healing.
Et se cist accident ne li vienent, si est li chose plus legiere.	If this accident does not occur, it is a lighter matter.
Et li cure si est que tu rewardes s’il i a aposteme chaut, si met sus l’espinee oile roset ou oile de moieuf d’uef, tant qu’il soit apaisiez;	 And the care is that if there is an abscess hot, apply oil of rose or oil from goose yolk until it is soothed.
puis met sus un des emplaustres confortans et sechans, et le lie d’un liien, et comande au malaide a reposer;	 Then place on one of the comforting and drying plasters and bandage with a tie, and command the patient to rest.
et ne dorme mie sus celle partie ou il sent la dolor, tant k’il soit sanez.	 And do not sleep on that part where he feels pain, until it is well.
Et se aucuns os se dessevre, si covient coper sus lou keur;	 And if any bone dislocates, then cover the area with a bandage;
et oste l’os, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, a une costure, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then extract the bone, then bring together the two lips of the wound, if large, with a stitch, then treat with fragrant balm ointment until it is well.
et se li chiés de l’os est brisiez, ki est apelez li «chiés de la kowe», se i boute ton pouchet de ta main senestre, et le met igal a l’autre main a ton pooir, puis met l’emplaustre et l’estele sus, se tu en a mestier;	 If the head of the joint is broken, called "the knee's head", put your poultice from your left hand and place it even with your right hand at will, then apply the plaster and stake on top if needed.
puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 Then bind it, and if there is bone exposed, treat above, below, and the wound until it is healed.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	Of broken bone of the hip joint
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	 Sometimes the hip bone breaks, and if this happens, there should be no slight reduction at all.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	 Treat long and down to the pubic bone, causing pain in place, swelling, and bruising where broken.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	 And the restoration is that you extend your hand above until it is over the breakage.
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	 And you say what the fracture and appearance of it is;
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	 If the fracture is only at the head, make the fracture even, until it returns to its natural shape.
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	;ta are and and: If you c.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	 And when you have made it even, place it on a board, then put a stake of wood or metal underneath, and hold the fracture so that it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	 And apply pressure from below the ribs until they are level.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And instruct the patient to sleep on their healthy side or back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	 If pus comes out, do not touch it, until the discharge is calmed down, and put what we have mentioned before.
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	 And then return to restoration, and hold it as needed, if there has been no further accident.
et c’est li maniere.	 And this is the manner.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	Of a fracture of the shoulder
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	 The adductors are those between the shoulder blade and the top of the shoulder, and if they are injured, then it should be restored according to one of two methods.
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	 which is that you take a piece of medium-sized bone in this form:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	 And cut two holes for the strings, and tie them at the top, then place the patient underneath.
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	 then pour the patient's arm that is broken on the bone piece until it heals, and provide them with a wooden brace at one-half its length, then fasten it below any heavy object or extenders as needed.
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	 then you must bind the fracture together with both hands at once, until the fracture heals properly.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a .ij. ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout .i. liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	; that theird; set sal the by; or d thembobint ou tue en lesse sulittelle est this is they.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	 And if you see that the extraction is further out, restrain the sinew below the break, and above the break, and stretch each muscle to its place.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	 And if the fracture is near the top of the shoulder, one must place a splint behind the socket and another on the other side, below the fracture.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	 And similarly if the fracture is on the other side, one must place a light splint without strain until the fracture is level with the socket and the bone.
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	 Then align the fracture as needed, and stabilize it unless an abscess occurs.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	 And if an abscess occurs, do not bind it until seven days have passed and apply a linen cloth soaked in oil of roses to ease the abscess.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	 Then bind it and the way to do so is to place a plaster over the fracture, then join the arm above the shoulder, placing your hand on the shoulder or breast.
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	 And put the sling on it, and hold above the shoulder, and along the arm, so that the arm is in its proper place if nothing prevents it, or if the bone is not moved.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	 And if you suspect that the bone is not moving, use splints, and place on the fracture a splint wider and stronger than others, and have between each splint an inch of space, and let each splint be so large that it passes the fracture by three inches from each side;
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	 Then hold onto the splints as I said at the beginning of this chapter on fractures, stronger and closer together.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	 And if you see the dislocation of the splints and the strain as we have said, during the hour when you return the fractured limb, and doubt that the wound is hot, let it be bound until the seventh day as we have said.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	 Then for three days observe the bandage, ensuring no itching or swelling occurs at the site, so that numbness cannot come to the limb because it is too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	 If necessary, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	 And if none of these incidents occur, do not dislocate it for more than three days or longer, and let the patient sleep on their back with their hands above their abdomen.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	 and place a linen bandage evenly on the shoulder socket, and watch every hour of the day or night to ensure that the broken limb does not move or become softened by the ties.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	 if it improves due to the power of medicine, and give the patient the flesh that we have previously prepared, in a way that the meat is most subtle.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	 And when it begins to resume, give it firm support.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	 And it is customary that the shoulder and leg should be reset in forty days altogether;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	 And then one must dislocate them again and administer baths and poultices with oil to realign the limb correctly.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	 And if the stricture is ugly and swollen, it remains dislocated for days or months.
de la brisure du bras	For a broken arm fracture
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	 The arm is made of two bones called "phalanges," one being small and the other supporting the palm.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	 and the other is large, and that which extends forward from the smaller joint.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	 Sometimes only the large phalange is broken, or the small one; sometimes both are fractured together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	 When the small phalanges are broken, the restoration and healing are easy;
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	 And when the large [bone] is broken, so it is bad healing, with more pain than when they were broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	 If it's only small vessels that are broken, then the treatment requires slight extension and balancing.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	 And if it's a fractured bone, then extraction must be done stronger;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	 And extend the hand near it, and tie up the sleeve higher than the others, and the small fingers lower than the other digits, and crosses of pain directly on him, and the bone in front of him raised higher, that the patient suffers no more trouble.
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	 Then extend the minor ministers both arms to the area under his hand or at the wrist, and other ministers another above.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	 And then place the mirror evenly, according to its best shape.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if in the break into pieces, place each one back to its position, and if any are dislocated that grip the bone, and you cannot restore it to its position, then strike above and cut the bone as we have said before.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	 And if with the fracture comes an open wound, I have spoken to each chapter separately;
si pren la cure.	 If you take this treatment.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	 And at the beginning of the restoration if an abscess arises, make a plaster from rose oil and white wax-based balm so that it is neither too hard nor too soft.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	 and apply the plaster gently over the area until the abscesses are calmed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	 And then remove the plaster, and put on a poultice with plenty of egg white, apply it where there are breaks, and make that patch wider and thicker than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	 and mark where there should be six or more additional splints in various arrangements:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	 whether the fracture is in one of the bones, or two.
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	 And is strained more towards the fracture than elsewhere, and every day less in approaching it, as I have said at the beginning of this chapter.
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	 And let the bandages that are on the fracture be soft and moist, and not hard or rough;
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	 And make the stitches to which it is fastened of flax, neither too thick nor too thin, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	 And repair the limb and ligament after some days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	 And if any accident comes to the limb, as itching that comes to the limb, then you must wash the limb with warm water until the itchiness is soothed.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	 and let the limb not rest too tightly.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	 And then resume the binding, and if the ligaments are softened and the bones set right, along with similar things, so it is.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if the swelling cannot come to the limb because it is too tight, you must soften it a bit and let it rest for some time until the swelling subsides, then resume binding.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	 And if none of these things that we have said comes to the patient, do not loosen until X days.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	 or in between, then secure its hands to its neck, and let their collars be equal, and guard against movement and shifting, and sleep on his back.
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	 And say that this fracture is healed in XYZ days or in XLV days, and sometimes in XX days, according to the composition and nature of the substances.
de la brisure de la main	Of a hand fracture
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	He says that on the back of the hand and in our fingers, there are few fractures, but they bend many times.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	 And when the plant of the hand is fractured or bent, it must be that the patient sews crosswise, and lies flat in front of him evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	 then places his hand under the extended table, and extends the physicians' fingers over the broken bones, and aligns them evenly until they are well joined.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	 and applies the plaster and poultices, if there is an abscess, then he puts in a splint according to the amount of the wound.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	 and it should be wrapped in a piece of linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	 And if the break is near the eyebrow within the belly of the sole, make a bandage from linen cloths and instruct the patient to fasten it at their injured arch.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	 Then the strain of a long bandage is applied and it should be adjusted just as large as the palm's sole, and the strain is maintained appropriately.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is in the hind part, it's necessary to place a splint underneath and another above on the plantar side, so that the hand remains exposed and straight; then bind it entirely around the hand, ensuring the ligaments between the two are sealed.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	 And if the break comes to either of your ankles, if they are swollen, adjust them equally as necessary.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	 and the strain with a sole is applied, and if you see that it requires a small straight splint to lift the fracture, do not move.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	 and if the break is like other ankles, in the index or one of the others, adjust them equally, and tie with the healthy toe that follows.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	 When you bind them all together firmly, so they do not move, or place on a pillow as if sewn.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	 And take care in the treatment and positioning of an abscess head, and remove what comes out as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	of a broken hip joint
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	 The bone of the hip is often broken, and it can be seen when it turns forward and backward;
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	 And its treatment involves binding the limbs above the breakage, and otherwise below.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	 The patient lies face downward, then each minister extends their link equally to their respective parts;
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	 And this is when the breakage occurs within the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	 If the fracture is near the root of the hip, let one ligament be towards the wrist and the other below the fracture.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	 And similarly if it's near the knee, then the links should be close to the knee and extensions below.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	 Then place the mirror on the bone, as evenly as in its natural shape with both hands, and then apply the bandage, and let it rest, if no abscess appears there.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	 And if an abscess is present, allow it to calm down first then return to your work and care;
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	 The ligature is made in the following manner.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	 It is necessary that you wrap it with two or three layers of doubled bandages and make allowance for excess material. Then bend the leg until the heel reaches the base of the calf, and insert a long thread between the thigh and the leg, below the groin, and let the end of the string pass over.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	 Then turn to the leg and thigh with a bandage, then apply it to the fracture site, and place a splint on the leg bone.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	 Then wrap the length between the leg and thigh with soft cloth to evenly apply pressure, then begin binding firmly using three or four twists above the fracture.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	 and as you move closer to the fracture site, less tighten it;
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	 then extend the two ends of the thread between the leg and thigh, and tie three more above that, then return to untie at the head end until you reach near the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	 If it doesn't move from its place while tightened, leave it as is; then if there are no signs of abscess or swelling appear.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	 If it occurs, if a dislocation happens, and quickly address what is happening, as we have said many times.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	 And if there are bone fragments involved, then cutting may be necessary, which one can do.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	 And if it cannot be done, then splitting the limb is required, and pulling out the iron.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	 And heal as we have said until it becomes sound again.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	 And never is the thigh broken so that one places stakes inside, as in the shoulder and arm.
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	 Yet, with such restoration performed, it does not harm the patient.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And know that the thigh is restored in one or two days, or a little more or less, depending on the variations of constitutions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	from the hollow of the knee joint
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	 It is said that in the glen of the neck there are few fractures, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	 And if broken, it is not so much a crack or piercing, but occurs in all wounds, and causes pain, and feels very unwell.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	 And the repair is that one aligns what was lost with its counterparts as much as possible, so they can move.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	 Then apply the plaster cast, and insert a round splint if necessary, and stabilize it as needed, then address all other breaks and injuries such as abscesses that are hot and similar issues.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then apply what is appropriate for each injury, ensuring they are well-tended.
de la brisure de la jambe	Concerning the breaking of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	 Know that in the leg there are two bones, one called the tibia and the other called the fibula.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	 and it experiences all types of fractures as they occur in the arm, so is the restoration just like that for the arm equally, and the procedures are all the same. And if both bones are broken together, turn the leg on all sides.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the delicate bone is shattered, then turn to face forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	 And if the large bone is broken, it causes great pain and the wound is visible.
et torne desoz.	 And then turn away from there.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	 Then make an extension, adjust it evenly, and attach the splints equally;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	 However, if the breakage is severe, and there are multiple fragments, the extension should be smaller and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	 and balance it according to your wisdom.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	 And when you have completed your work, take two staves of hardwood that encircle the leg from one side and the other, being double the length of the leg from knee to ankle.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	 then wrap it twice with bands above and below, securely tie them together, and at this band the leg will not lean to the right or left, which is well.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	 And none administer the bear's gall of the long leg bone, and if it is broken, and they set the leg to prevent movement, properly performing the splint in the break where there is injury.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	 And move each day the leg, to see if there is an abscess or any other accident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If treated until it becomes healthy again.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Regarding the fracture of the bone of the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle there is no fracture, but at the bone of the foot a break occurs sometimes and in the shinbone, and nothing happens to cause weakness or other conditions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	 And if it occurs as a broken foot bone fracture and you see the bones protruding from each other, place such maladies underfoot on the ground, as if they would walk, then now put your own foot beneath theirs where the bones are raised, and press until they return to their places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	 First place the plug and stop up above it, then put under the belly with two fingers a small tablet of hemp paste, then strain towards the abdomen immediately, then wrap all around with bandages and other things as needed.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, you will loosen the ligament, for you will find that the bones are equal again, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	 And if there are any broken bones, repair them, as we have said about the hand's bones.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	 Then insert a splint for the broken bone according to its length, and make it slightly wider, then place underneath the abdomen that tablet I mentioned, and strain immediately.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	 And if there are two or three, or more broken bones, repair them and place a splint for each according to its quantity, wrapped in one linen cloth, and strain the tablet underneath the abdomen.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	 And so it is when on top of the table near the head of the bed, that you should properly position him well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	 And one must not forget the other things I have said about other fractures, just as we have mentioned.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	 and treat each accident as it is due.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	Regarding the fracture of the hand bone
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	 When the bone of womanhood is broken, she should be placed in an enlarged seat, then tilt to the part of her back and held behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	 then fill the bag with cotton from the patient's nature, and put as much in as it can hold.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	 then stand the woman up and lift her back little by little, and then push in the cotton until it comes to the entrance of the nature, and aligns the bone with its natural position.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	 And when it is about to urinate, wrap with cotton, and after having urinated, if it resets itself, thus make seven days or so.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	 If it is healed, and if you see this, take a sheeps' bladder, tie cloth to the opening, and pour all the contents into nature.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	 Then blow through the cloth until the inside of the bladder is empty.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	 Nature will restore the fracture;
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then be filled with cotton and leave so for several days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	 And when the bone of the arm or woman's body is broken, restore it as we have said in the thigh bone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	 And these fractures are not hidden from those who apply their study and effort to it; listen to my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	 For the fracture indicates various pathways for restoration in several cases.
enten le donques.	 Then let us proceed.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	 In the rod, when it is broken, it takes an oatmeal shape and inserts the rod.
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	 Then wrap with a dressing around it, and leave for three days or as needed on it, and it will be healed quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	Of fracture with a wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for those who have a fracture with a wound, especially if it is large like the bone of the hip or shoulder or similar, to be healed now, as long as the sinews we mentioned confirm this.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound is healed, and there remains lead poisoning, unless you have other things, then begin to restore the fracture in that same hour or day, as long as abscesses do not appear.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	; they can. the same:
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is visible above the joint, it must be gently set into place with your hands, in slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	 And if the extension does not fit to make your hands equal, use this instrument of iron which is 7 or 8 inches long, and its width corresponds to the size of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	 and therefore you will need your barber to grasp it 3 or 4 times, depending on what is needed for each breakage treatment.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	 and make it round and slightly thick, so that it does not bend under the pressure on the limb during your work, and leave some room at the front end.
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	 And it is called "palanquin," so that the shoulder head must be placed under the visible part of the bone.
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	 And he must set it once so that it returns to its place, ensuring they are equal on either side.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	 And if the fracture is subtle, and the splints cannot properly take hold of the bone, then it must be cut off until the splints have power.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	 And if you cannot return the bone as we have said, use the handle of an appropriate instrument for this purpose, either cutting or sawing, to your ability.
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	 then remove that which is embedded in the bone with a sharp and small scrapes.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	 And when the bone is returned to its place, if the patient feels great pain afterwards, believe that it is not in its natural position.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	 If you do so that it returns to its place, then wrap the wound in a fine black sticky pitch, and neatly if necessary.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	 and do not put any salve or other substance on the wound that may contain oil, so as to prevent decay.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	 then apply dressings as you have restored the beone, and leave the wound exposed, bandage the covering completely, according to the size of the wound, and ensure well that the wound is not strained with the fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	 And many times have foolish physicians done this to patients, causing them harm or death on numerous occasions.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	 So it is the application less harsh and more gentle than other fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	 And if the wound is bad or large and you suspect no accident has occurred here as we have said, and there is pain at the location, then it does not require placing on a bed of eggshells.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	 but wrap around it, in place of eggshells, with durable fabrics and bind them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	 And when you see after one or two days that pus flows from the wound, remove what you have placed on it, and apply healing salve to the wounds, as with a four-part remedy and similar substances.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it is necessary to loosen the limb twice a day, in the morning and evening, until it becomes relaxed and healthy.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the limb be fitted with a splint so that the bow supports it lightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if several days pass and it cannot be straightened but continues bent like this, for there are small bone fragments, you must clean the wound with gauze and remove all those unnecessary fragments that cause pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	 And if an abscess comes to the area, or another form of decay, it is necessary that you treat it, as described in this chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	 And when the bone is fractured and protrudes from the limb, as in the hip or shoulder, with other similar large limbs, do not attempt to pull it out, for many times this leads to death, but leave it until it heals.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	 By chance it may occur through him after twenty or thirty days, then treat the wound if you know how.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	 and if you do not know how, leave it alone.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	From bruises which arise upon the saddle.
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	 We often come after the healing of the fracture, especially when it is near the joint, and an unpleasant thing to see is how the limb is shaped.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	 and perhaps cannot perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	 Thus beware if it feels fresh:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	 if you administer medicines like aloes, incense, myrrh, and frankincense, among others, then take any of these things individually or all together, and boil them with tonic wine, vinegar abundance, or vinegar essence.
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	 And the metal is inserted into the nostrils, and it is tightened well, and should not be loosened for days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	 Then dislocate it again, and repeat with another one until there are no more bone fragments.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	 or you strain over a well-made piece of wood;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	 for the property of the wood is such that it draws out all swelling on top of limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	 and if the bone fragment is as hard as stone and needs to be removed, do so with a saw, and create the excess visible.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 or you reduce it by any means necessary until it is removed, and heal as long as it remains clean.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	A limb which is weak after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	 When the broken bone is restored, and follows after weak and delicate limbs for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	 Because one is too tightly bound, and was not loosened as it should be.
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	 Or because there were too many bindings, and could not come to relieve the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	 Or due to excessive bleeding;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	 Or because of overly large movements, not at the right time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	 Or because it has little blood in its body, so is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	 And the treatment should be that you feed the patient well and make the body tender until there is an increase in blood within him.
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	 And administer baths, and give joy and comfort to him.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	 Then apply poultices to the limb, such that it draws significant nourishment, and often raises its temperature with water compresses until proper nourishment reaches the limb.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	 And returns to its natural position.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	After injury has healed, the limb becomes twisted
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	 When the member is twisted after restoration, and the bone is broken openly, and the shape of the limb is unattractive, yet it still maintains its natural function.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	 If you do not trust the foolish who claim that the limb should be broken anew entirely, and many fools in our land have done so.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	 And these treatments are blamed, leading to great harm, and possibly death.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	 However, if the lumps and tortures are recent, it is necessary to treat them with hot water, or boiled softening herbs such as witch hazel leaves, roots, melilotus seeds, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	 Et you apply the soothing paste like diachylon well made, and take the mucilage of wormwood, and mix it with fat from geese or oil of sesame, and make a poultice on top.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	 And you take the animal fats, and grind them with fine bran, and add certain medicines that reduce swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	 And at no time is an inflamed bone treated by continuously rubbing with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	 And thus, adjust the position of each limb.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	 And if the tortuousness is old and hardened, like stone, and it needs to be pried open with iron, so that you must cover it completely with a slightly sharp scalpel.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	 and apply compresses and pay attention during treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs, if necessary now reset without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	 For if delayed, the eyes may become inflamed, and possibly it can be returned to place with difficulty.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	 For this is why it must not be moved when it has swelled.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	 Many times, it brings about phlegm and other pains.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	 Also, when this occurs, have the patient drink wine, then let them rest until the swelling is calmed.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	 Then apply warm water and oil to the limb, then gently massage each part as treatment comes into place in its proper location.
