Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	.
des mandibules	Of the jawbones
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	 Occasionally, the jawbones may be dislocated, and dislocations of both occur in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	 or they are slightly out of place from their original positions, and soften a little.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	 or they are entirely dislocated and tilt towards the painful side, causing drooling from the mouth that they cannot contain, nor can they close their mouth, which also wraps around their tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When dislocation is slight, it can return on its own in various positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	 If it is complete and well-formed, then one must quickly reset it without delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	 And in such a manner that the minister washes your head and inserts a small spoon into one of his hands at the root of the lower jaw's dislocation inside the mouth, if the dislocation is from two parts.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	 And let the other hand be ready to balance it out.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	 Instruct the patient to relax his jawbones and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And then put it inside of its place until they are balanced equally; and take your right beforehands:
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	 And if the resetting is difficult, especially if both jawbones are together, use warm water and oil to gently move them.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	 Do not attempt the reset otherwise as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	 And when they are returned equally, and the patient's mouth closes well indicating softening sensation, then place on cloths soaked in a padded cover made of rose oil and wax, and lightly bind with loose ties.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	 and the patient sleeps on his back with his head between two pillows, ensuring he does not move to either side or strain to shift, but gently eats soft meat until the pains have subsided, and the jawbones are numbed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	 and then provide him what he wants to eat easily, and do not work at opening the mouth for eating or drinking until his jawbones are well numbed and soothed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two jawbones cannot be reset to their place within an hour and are not returned to their original positions, fever and usual complaints may come, and perhaps abdominal issues, or possibly complete vomiting of bile alone.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	 And when you see this, then you know it is dislocation.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	 and many times death occurs to those who experience it, within nine days.
de la forcelle	Of the hernia
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The hernia cannot dislodge from within the ribcage and below, and it is never displaced once formed, and one feels it well.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	 And the restoration is such that the patient lies on their back with legs apart, and extends their arms.
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	 and then press firmly at its place with your hand, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	 then apply the plaster and bandage, and strain (or tighten).
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	 and the shoulder that is towards the armpit cannot dislocate.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	 if not possible, and if it does dislocate at any time, then reset to its place as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then apply the plaster and bandage, and strain (or tighten), and advise the patient to rest until they are well again.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	 And similarly, bring back the head of the shoulder when it has moved out of its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Regarding the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	 Know that the shoulder is dislocated in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	 by which one is that it dislocates to the bottom part of the upper arm;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	 and the second is towards the lower part;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	 and sometimes upwards, but this occurs rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	 and it does not dislocate backwards from the shoulder, nor inward into the muscles.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	 and sometimes downwards towards the upper arm, especially in those who have little flesh, as it happens quickly to them.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	 but for those with ample flesh, it comes out scarcely, and returns slightly.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes there are individuals with blows or fractures, and their shoulder swells with a hot abscess; they think it is dislocated due to this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	 Indeed, you must test it, until you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	 And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	 And dislocation is known when it moves towards the shoulder blade, and there is a noticeable difference between the affected and healthy shoulders, and you will find their various manifestations.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	 and at the top of the shoulder, you will find a hollow, as if it were an eye socket.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	 and the patient cannot return their hand to its normal position or move at all.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	 and similarly, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden, for you can clearly observe it at the socket.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	 and this type of dislocation cannot be corrected unless it occurs anew or if the child is ill.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	 And the method is for the minister to lift the patient's hand upward, then place his hands under the shoulder, and firmly lift the dislocation back into position.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	 And the minister lifts the hand, and extends it upwards, then places it below.
si venra hastanment.	 if done quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	 And if it does not come as we have said on the following days, then it is necessary for the patient to be bathed in warm water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	 and it should be treated with soothing and calming substances such as an infusion of valerian and fenugreek and honey in water, then treated.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	 then place a strip of linen equally not too soft nor too hard on the patient's back under the shoulder blade, then align their heel with the strip, and gently lift the head of the dislocated shoulder.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	 And other remedies apply to the patient's head, so it does not move downward.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	 and when that shoulder returns now, you see if you reset according to this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	 and ensure that a physician who is taller than the patient is present.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	 and stand on the side of their chest, push up the shoulder from under the seat of the patient, lift the seat to the top, so that the patient hangs in the air.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	 and other remedaders guide the hand of the patient downward toward their belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	 If the patient is too lightweight, accompany them with something heavy, and the dislocation returns now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	 And the reset can also be done in another way.
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	 and it is that you plant a long pole into the ground so that the head of the shoulder is aligned as with a spit, neither too thick nor too thin.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	 Then it is to be put back under the patient, but that he has soft cloths over, and the patient lies long on his side.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	 Then extend his hand towards the other side gently, and the joint will return to its place quickly.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	 And if it does not wish to return for all these reasons that we have mentioned, then do this remedy:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	 Take a shing of two arms in length and four fingers wide, which has the head turned so that it can enter evenly from under the seat, as follows:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	 Then place soft cloths on top of his side so that it does not slip the patient, then put under the seat where the patient lies.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	 Extend his arm over the length of his side, and place the shoulder on top, with the hand at the head of the arm, then put the arm under an arbor of a wide stool, extend the hands downward, and let the body hang towards the other side.
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	 The joint has been dislocated for some time now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is set in place, however you do so, it must be that you put under the saddle a staff of woolen yarn, then apply a poultice of powdered medicine, with incense and ointment of frankincense on all around the shoulder, then tighten it away from the saddle quickly, and wrap the hand at its neck, leaving hands hanging thus.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	 And it is necessary that he rests little by little, until the limb is comfortable, because it will recover sooner.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	 and then rest more after 3 or 7 days and move it;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	 and if it is firm and not weakened, then healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	 And if the joint is forced out due to moisture that caused it or another reason, you must apply three punctures with cautery as described in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	 And if you do all this and it dislocates again after e7 days, and the joint does not hold, and cannot lift any arm upwards, then understand that the nerve at the top of the shoulder is pinched or stretched or weakened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	 and know that the joint will never be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	 The dislocation that is towards the worse and the muscles or back, it occurs due to impact and extension of hands, and by another method.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And care until it becomes healthy again.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing come tremors in the limb and later movements, the patient uses them many times until those tremors cease, returning to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	Of the dislocation of the knee
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	 Seams that the shoulder joint is dislocated to points, and returns to its point of dislocation.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	 And it is dislocated from all parts, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation is not properly reset, as one can see clearly and feel distinctly.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	 And it is dislocated according to each type of displacement.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	 And when joining the patient's joint properly with the healthy one, you should see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	 For the joint is raised and cannot bend the arm or reach its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	 And you must reset it immediately as abscesses appear, for if they arise, the repositioning would be more difficult.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	 and perhaps cannot be realigned at all in some cases, especially when it is behind.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	 if worse than other types of dislocation, causes more pain, and possibly leads to death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	 And restoration is possible when it can be realigned, you extend your hands on both sides of the limb.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	 and spread the arms wide, placing the hands around it as indicated by its circumference, above and below, and pushing the joint back together or at the base of the palm until it returns to its original position.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	When dislocation is before, it returns when the hand doubles to itself and the root of the palm's edge that has been dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	 And if it does not return to its place, perform strong straightening.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	 And there are two ministers who extend the arm and support it with their hands, so that it does not move during extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	 Then turn the arm from each side, then wrap a long and wide piece of cloth around it.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	 And when the wind reaches the joint at its connection to the hand, anoint it with any oil to soften the joint, then bind the joint firmly until it heals.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	 And when it is in place, put on dry paste with egg yolk, then bind it firmly, and support the arm at the sore patient's neck, and leave it for some days, then unbind it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	 And if the joint is firmly in place, then dislocate it again and leave it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	 And if you see that the joint does not tighten well, then repeat the manipulation and reposition it, leaving it so for a few days until it is firmly set.
puis le deslie.	 Then dislocate again.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	 And if it feels weak after the resetting of the joint and moves again, then bathe and rub well, pressing until it is eased.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	 or you place a fat sheep's wool on the joint, then leave it for a day and a night, then reset it, and have the patient take a bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	 and when it is sweaty, rub the joint gently, then replace the sheep's wool on top, and then have the patient bathe.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And thus do so twice or three times until it is put back in place.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	 and if you see, then apply a warm wheat paste mixed with butter, and strain over it.
si revenra a sa disposition.	 so it shall return to its proper place.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	 The hand's dislocation occurs, and its return is easier than other dislocations.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	 Nevertheless, it must be quickly returned to its place at the same hour as it is dislocated, so that it may swell or an abscess may form hotly.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	 And the resettling is that you place the injured hand under a table, extend its fingers, and align the wrists equally so that it places its palm over the dislocation's appearance, and hold until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	 It is also necessary to check if it is properly positioned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	 Then instruct the patient to place their back on a table for extension and retraction.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	 If the dislocation is on the back of the hand, make the patient place their hand's back against a table, and let the doctor position their hand under the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	 If it returns now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	 If not, apply the soothing touch of asterisked straps and let them rest until they start to ease again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	 And if it cannot be tolerated, and you cannot place it back in position for several days, as the twisted joint persists.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	 and neither providing food nor water to the patient until their hands are sufficiently healed, and they can grip nothing at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	 then tell that the nerves or the artery have been cut.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	 If there is no other remedy than to apply fire near the wound, and sometimes it serves no other purpose.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hands are at rest, place them on the platform as we have said, then grasp and leave for 5 days, then release and let it be so.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if they cannot move well, and there is no trembling, then apply warm water with millet, and rub until it feels fine.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	Of dislocation of the hand's fingers
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	 Dislocations never occur in both directions of the hand, neither to the back of the palm nor to the belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	 Then they are stuck in place, and the dislocation is returned to its pockets until it heals, then support the head of the hand and turn it towards the part where it is dislocated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	 And leave it for two days, then set it straight again after that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	 and from there bind it as we have said, leaving the joint for a day, then making it move again, and rejoining the nut.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and do this often until it is narrowed, and do the same if dislocated to the belly of the hand, and do as you did before, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	 And likewise do, when it is dislocated from another side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	For the dislocation of the spinal column in the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spinal column or the neck is dislocated, if there are multiple occurrences and no remedy, it quickly kills the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	 And the signs are such that the discharges jump up forcefully without willingness and cannot be held back, causing many times any limb to become weakened or affecting either both knees or one of the two arms or a single one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	 And often it moves the spine into four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	 That which moves to the rear is called "gilbo-itis":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	 The treatment is that you should beware if "gilbo-itis" arises from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	 If there is no remedy or healing for the entirety of it.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	 And that which comes from falling or impacts or similar things are the ancient methods of treatment with great words, where there is no benefit in all.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	 However, I have shortened it according to my intention, and formed remedies in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	 I say that in the swelling that comes upon the breast, there is neither remedy nor health;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	 and also those that arise directly in the ribs, and cannot be treated except for those precisely which come to the back, as I say;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	 and it is that the sick person be stretched over their face one place evenly, and have strain from them, so they do not writhe;
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	 then apply a hot iron to the head in clay formed, and another at the feet, and tie a bandage around the neck of the sick person, and another at the hips, and at the knees, and ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	 And two ministers know the ligaments, one at the top and the other at the joints, among the two sharpened instruments.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	 And they should be well secured, and position the instrument as we have said, with his palms on the spine forming a straight line until it is properly aligned.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	 And if it does not return with this procedure, take a stick three arms long and sharpened from the front, and place the patient to one side, then set the head of the stick at the front above their pelvis, and then insert the middle part of the stick into the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	 And position the minister's hands on the other end of the stick and press firmly until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	 And if you see it, make it with a turnkey that turns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	 And you should insert two wires through the head of the arm with great swelling, and toward other parts, and between each wire, there should be enough space.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	 And in each wire, the turnkey must fit correctly, and the wires should be firmly secured in place, so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	 And between each wire there should be an additional turning wire where the links can turn, and in these turns two small wires of enough length to rotate the turnkey.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	 And then secure the link among the elements on the turnkey toward the head, and the other link towards the extremities at the other turnkey, and each servant rotates their turnkey along the entire chain, and the master aligns the spine as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 When they are aligned, place the drying plaster with plenty of wax, then the cotton, and then the splint from a tablet three fingers long to properly position the glenoid cavity and the healthy part of the spondyle, then bind it with a ligament as we have said, and let the patient rest quietly until healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	 If no issue arises by the end of healing, administer softening and soothing medications with the splint we have mentioned previously.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	 And never administer a piece of iron, and ensure that there is no appearance in the back part of the spinal column, and take care to avoid dislocations.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	 And it is the bone that has opened up, which is why there must be no assumption.
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	 There might come death by chance.
des dislocations de la hainche	Dislocation of the hip joint
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	 Understand that the joints of the hip and shoulder only come from dislocation alone, not like other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	 and the joint of the hip is dislocated in four ways:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	 into itself and outward, and front and back;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	 and more internally than externally, and rarely dislocates front and back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	 And the recognition of an internal dislocation is such that when one joins the injured leg with the healthy one, it becomes longer and opens up more joints for the injured than the healthy, and the injured cannot double its knee at fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	 And it is the leg which is near an inflamed abscess due to the fact that the hip joint approaches there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of those for whom it occurs is that this accident is contrary to those before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	 And for those who suffer from it in front, they should keep their leg extended properly according to recovery.
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	 In any case, do not double the pain in the neck, and if you wish to make it move beforehand, it cannot be done, and retains its urine, and swells with anger, and as it moves forward, passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs for those who suffer behind it are such that they cannot expand their knee or double it, and the leg is more twisted than the other, anger is alleviated, and the head of the hip to its place below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	 The return of this type of dislocation is that you should reset it where the dislocation occurred first, and it remains according to its position, there is no treatment.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	 and it must not be assumed to have healed.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	 And in cases where the dislocation is recent, and it's one of the four types of dislocations, you should quickly return the joint, push down on it and pull upwards, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	 By chance if it returns, no further treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	 And if it does not return in this manner, you must select a strong minister and bind the leg firmly with two hands or one band around the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	 and another minister extends his hands over it in such a way that he places them below the kneecaps, then tightens a thin band around the thigh.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	 and another cuts the head off the sling.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	 and all extend upwards and downwards at once so that the patient is lifted from the ground once and hangs suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for 4 types, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is fine.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	 If not, you must apply treatment to its kindred.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	 When dislocation is in the jawbone, you must support the patient on their sound side and then place a band around the base of the thigh, and the part that is below the groin, then extend the band upwards towards the groin and towards the hip.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	 Then gather other ministers of men by their arms, and embrace the large joint of the crooked thigh, extending it forward fully.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	 If it returns to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	 And this manner of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	 And if you cannot hold it in the manner we have said, then one must bind the two feet of the crooked leg together with a strong flexible ligature above both heels and knees, and keep the affected leg extended further than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	 Then hang it from the head of a staff, with two long arms outstretched on the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	 Then command one minister to embrace the head of the thigh, and have other ministers hang alongside with the crooked leg, fully embracing the thigh, as now the joint quickly returns.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	 And when the dislocation is on its way out, you should place the patient as mentioned in those with gangrenous wounds, and properly separate the ligaments above the affected leg, and at the knee likewise.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	 Then apply two cauterizing agents: one on the head and one elsewhere on the body, then insert a cauterizing rod between the buttocks near the affected area.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	 And have moistened bandages placed around it so that the patient does not move, then each minister moves towards him and he aligns his hand with the dislocation equally.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 If it returns, that is well.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If not, place on a board and press as we have said with sprains, and touch the patient near the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	 And when the dislocation is in front, it must be that you extend the affected leg quickly, and according to what I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	 And place his hand on the painful side of the affected area, then press with the other hand and extend towards the groin.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	 If the dislocation is in its place, do not extend the patient's arm or lift it off the ground. Instead, let it lie as if the elbow were dislocated when it was set wrongly during sleep on both elbows, as we have said above.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	 And let the ligament be stretched as we have described beforehand, and one must apply pressure to the joint against the board.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	 And it will reach a point when the patient extends his legs, which will be equal.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	 Then approach the buttocks and place the splint, and secure with a bandage so that the elbow does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	 And let it rest for three or four days, then release it, and place the splint again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	 And if you see that they are equal, then strain as before, and let it be for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Then release it gently, and allow the limb to heal completely, until the member is comforted.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of shoulder dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	 The joint dislocates in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	 that is to say, inward and outward, and backward.
et ne desalue point devant.	 and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	 And the signs are such that you command the patient to bend his leg at the hip, and if it does not return to the hip, understand that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	 and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright straight, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back to his face, and put your foot under his.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	 Then take its thighs with your palms, and pull them apart between your thumbs, then bend the two shanks of the thigh firmly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	 and other ministers extend their foot, until the kneecap returns to its place, with signs that it bends well on its thigh slightly.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	 and apply the plaster over it, straighten the leg at the hip, with bandages firm for three or four days, then release.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 and do not make the patient walk too soon until their limb is healed.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not much affected, it must be firmly supported strongly, as we have said in the treatment of the elbow, until it becomes well-aligned.
de la dislocation dou talon	Regarding ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes numb, never fully dislocated, within and without.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	 And signs are such that the ankle is swollen, and try before reaching the part from where it dislocates.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 The repositioning should be gentle, and he must stretch it lightly into his hands when barely touched.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	 When it is dislocated completely, one must make the patient sit upright directly and gently move the limb using a staff outside through the leg above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	 Then raise the foot towards your right hand, and then towards the left two times, then extend it upwards, and place the foot firmly above.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	 And do this twice as we have said, bending and extending the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	 If it returns, that is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	 If not, repeat the procedure since it returns.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	 If it cannot return this way, make the patient lie on their back on the ground and firmly press a staff between their thighs, with linens around them so they do not shake.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	 Then dye the minister's thigh, and another minister extends his foot with ropes or strips of cloth so that he ties them around the neck of the foot.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	 Then each minister is extended equally, and the ties are pulled tight between their thighs to hold the patient steady as they stretch them.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 Then place the mirror symmetrically for the dislocation at his hands, and another minister dyes the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return rapidly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	 And when it reaches the point of no return, apply the poultice and plug thereon, strain firmly, tie the foot to the leg, and watch for the veins behind the ankle that the ties are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	 Then let it rest for two or three days, and if he improves, bind it loosely.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	 Then remove the bandage on the fourth day or sooner, and forbid the patient from moving for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And if he improves before this time, it is not assured that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes there, one must soothe it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	From the shoulder dislocation and its treatment, let's discuss a few related matters:
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	by;t what d. If:
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	 And if the dislocation is in any of his shoulder or foot bones, it is fitting that you make the patient sit on a level surface or a table straight up, and place your foot under the joints affected, then press firmly with your foot until they return.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	 And when they are even, and nothing appears amiss, place two fingers of your foot under the sole and strain firmly, then let it rest for three days before removing.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And make it rest until it is set right.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	For both wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	 When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one sees that it needs to be restored, often happens that the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	 If you are not overly confident in the treatment, unless you are wise in the art and have practiced it for a long time, and if you are compassionate and merciful and slow to judge;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	 And begin with soothing treatments for hot abscesses, and leave the patient in God's hand if you do not see hope of health.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	 And when you see hope, then reset the limb to its place now, so that the abscess may heal there.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	 And when the limb is in place, then apply soothing treatments for hot abscesses and care for the wound as needed with dry ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	 And with the dislocation there is a break, and small bones will be displaced, and treat them as we have described in simple illnesses.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 And be wary of succumbing to fear, as I have advised, for it is fitting according to your Maker and the wisdom of armament and body.
